# ActiveCampaign

Email marketing, marketing automation, and CRM tools you need to create incredible customer experiences.

## Actions

### Create Contact

Creates a new contact.

#### Parameters
- **email**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **firstName**: `Text`

- **lastName**: `Text`

- **phone**: `Text`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "activecampaign",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "activecampaign_create_contact",
    "input": {
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Update Contact

Updates an existing contact.

---


### Subscribe or Unsubscribe Contact From List

Subscribes a Contact to a List it is not currently associated with, or Unsubscribes a Contact from a list is currently associated with.

---


### Add Tag to Contact

Adds a tag to contact.

---


### Add Contact to Account

Adds a contact to an ActiveCampaign account.

---


### Create Account

Creates a new account.

#### Parameters
- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **accountUrl**: `Text`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "activecampaign",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "activecampaign_create_account",
    "input": {
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "accountUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Update Account

Updates an account.

---

## Triggers

### New Campaign Bounce

Triggers when a contact email address bounces from a sent campaign.

---


### New Deal Task

Triggers when a new deal task is created.

---


### New Deal Added or Updated

Triggers when a new deal is created or existing deal is updated.

---


### New or Updated Account

Triggers when a new account is added or an existing account’s details are updated

---


### Updated Contact

Triggers when an existing contact details are updated.

---


### New Contact Task

Triggers when a new contact task is added.

---


### Deal Task Completed

Triggers when a deal task has been completed.

---


### New Contact Note

Triggers when a new contact note is added.

---


### Tag Added or Removed From Contact

Triggers when a a Tag is added or removed from a Contact

---


### New Campaign Link Click

Triggers when a contact clicks a link in a campaign message (will only run once for each unique link).

---


### New Deal Note

Triggers when a new deal note is created.

---




# Actual Budget

Personal finance app

## Actions

### Import Transaction

Add a transaction

#### Parameters
- **account_id**: `Text`
  ID of the account you want to import a transaction to
  **Required**: Yes

- **date**: `DateTime`
  Date the transaction took place
  **Required**: Yes

- **payee_name**: `Text`
  Name of the payee

- **amount**: `Number`
  The dollar value of the transaction

- **category**: `Text`
  ID of the transaction category

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the transaction

- **imported_id**: `Text`
  Unique ID given by the bank for importing

- **transfer_id**: `Text`
  ID of the transaction in the other account for the transfer

- **cleared**: `Boolean`
  Flag indicating if the transaction has cleared or not

- **imported_payee**: `Text`
  Raw description when importing, representing the original value

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "actual-budget",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "import_transaction",
    "input": {
      "account_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "date": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "payee_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "amount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "category": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "imported_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "transfer_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cleared": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "imported_payee": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Get Budget

Get your monthly budget

#### Parameters
- **month**: `StaticDropdown`
  The month of the budget you want to get
  **Required**: Yes

- **year**: `StaticDropdown`
  The year of the budget you want to get
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "actual-budget",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_budget",
    "input": {
      "month": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "year": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Import Transactions

Import Transactions

#### Parameters
- **account_id**: `Text`
  ID of the account you want to import a transaction to
  **Required**: Yes

- **transactions**: `JSON`
  A json array of the transaction object
  Default value: `[{"payee_name":`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "actual-budget",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "import_transactions",
    "input": {
      "account_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "transactions": "[{\"payee_name\":"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Get Accounts

Get your accounts

---


### Get Categories

Get your categories

---

```json
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "acumbamail_create_subscriber_list",

      "listname": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

# Afforai

Helps you search, summarize, and translate knowledge from hundreds of documents to help you produce trustworthy research.

## Actions

### Ask Chatbot

You can find Chatbot ID by clicking settings button under **Actions** for given chatbot.

#### Parameters
- **sessionID**: `Text`
  You can find Chatbot ID by clicking settings button under **Actions** for given chatbot.
  **Required**: Yes

- **history**: `Array`
  **Required**: Yes

- **role**: `StaticDropdown`
  The role of the message sender.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | user | 'user' |
  | assistant | 'assistant' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **content**: `Text`
  The content of the message.
  **Required**: Yes

- **powerful**: `Boolean`
  **Required**: Yes

- **google**: `Boolean`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "afforai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "afforai_ask_chatbot",
    "input": {
      "sessionID": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "history": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "role": "'user'",
      "content": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "powerful": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "google": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# AI Answer
## Actions

### Create Phone Call

Create a phone call to customer from Agent

#### Parameters
- **agentID**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **phoneNumber**: `Text`
  Enter the phone number, along with country code, in format (e.g., +919876543210
  **Required**: Yes

- **details**: `Object`
  Optional details with key-value pairs (e.g., customer_id, priority

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ai-answer",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createPhoneCall",
    "input": {
      "agentID": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phoneNumber": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "details": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Schedule Call Agent

Schedule a call with an agent

#### Parameters
- **agentID**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **phoneNumber**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **executionTime**: `Text`
  Time to schedule the call in YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS format.
  **Required**: Yes

- **timezone**: `Text`
  Timezone of the scheduled call (e.g., Asia/Calcutta
  **Required**: Yes

- **prospectDetails**: `Object`
  Optional prospect details with key-value pairs (e.g., customer_id, priority

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ai-answer",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "scheduleCallAgent",
    "input": {
      "agentID": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phoneNumber": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "executionTime": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "timezone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "prospectDetails": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Amazon S3

Scalable storage in the cloud

## Actions

### Upload File

Upload an File to S3

#### Parameters
- **file**: `File`
  **Required**: Yes

- **fileName**: `Text`
  my-file-name (no extension

- **acl**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | private | 'private' |
  | public-read | 'public-read' |
  | public-read-write | 'public-read-write' |
  | authenticated-read | 'authenticated-read' |
  | aws-exec-read | 'aws-exec-read' |
  | bucket-owner-read | 'bucket-owner-read' |
  | bucket-owner-full-control | 'bucket-owner-full-control' |

- **type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | image/png | 'image/png' |
  | image/jpeg | 'image/jpeg' |
  | image/gif | 'image/gif' |
  | audio/mpeg | 'audio/mpeg' |
  | audio/wav | 'audio/wav' |
  | video/mp4 | 'video/mp4' |
  | application/pdf | 'application/pdf' |
  | application/msword | 'application/msword' |
  | text/plain | 'text/plain' |
  | application/json | 'application/json' |
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "amazon-s3",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "upload-file",
    "input": {
      "file": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "fileName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "acl": "'private'",
      "type": "'image/png'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Read File

Read a file from S3 to use it in other steps

#### Parameters
- **key**: `Text`
  The key of the file to read
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "amazon-s3",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "read-file",
    "input": {
      "key": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

## Triggers

### New File

Trigger when a new file is uploaded.

#### Parameters
- **folderPath**: `Text`

#### Example
```json
{
  "trigger": {
    "valid": true,
    "type": "POLLING",
    "settings": {
      "folderPath": null
    }
  }
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

---

# Apify

Your full‑stack platform for web scraping

## Actions

### Start an Apify Actor

Starts an Apify Actor web scraper

#### Parameters
- **actorid**: `Text`
  The id of the Actor to run [Use either id, or the username then ~ then the name] (compulsory
  **Required**: Yes

- **jsonbody**: `JSON`
  The JSON input to pass to the Actor [you can get the JSON from a run in your Apify account]. If left blank will use defaults. (optional
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "apify",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "startActor",
    "input": {
      "actorid": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "jsonbody": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# AssemblyAI

Transcribe and extract data from audio using AssemblyAI's Speech AI.

## Actions

### Search words in transcript

Search through the transcript for keywords. ' + 'You can search for individual words, numbers, or phrases containing up to five words or numbers.

---


### Delete transcript

Remove the data from the transcript and mark it as deleted.

---


### Transcribe

Transcribe an audio or video file using AssemblyAI.

---


### Get Transcript Redacted Audio

Get the result of the redacted audio model.

---


### Get Transcript

Retrieves a transcript by its ID.

---


### List transcripts

Retrieve a list of transcripts you created. Transcripts are sorted from newest to oldest. The previous URL always points to a page with older transcripts.

---


### Get Transcript Sentences

Retrieve the sentences of the transcript by its ID.

---


### Get Transcript Subtitles

Export the transcript as SRT or VTT subtitles.

#### Parameters
- **id**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **format**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | SRT | 'srt' |
  | VTT | 'vtt' |
  Default value: `'srt'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **chars_per_caption**: `Number`
  The maximum number of characters per caption

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "assemblyai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "getSubtitles",
    "input": {
      "id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "format": "'srt'",
      "chars_per_caption": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Azure OpenAI

Powerful AI tools from Microsoft

## Actions

### Ask GPT

The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion depending on the model. Don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Parameters
- **deploymentId**: `Text`
  The name of your model deployment.
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.
  Default value: `0.9`

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion depending on the model. Don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text
  Default value: `2048`
  **Required**: Yes

- **topP**: `Number`
  An alternative to sampling with temperature, called nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered.
  Default value: `1`

- **frequencyPenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far, decreasing the model's likelihood to repeat the same line verbatim.
  Default value: `0`

- **presencePenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far, increasing the mode's likelihood to talk about new topics.
  Default value: `0.6`

- **memoryKey**: `Text`
  A memory key that will keep the chat history shared across runs and flows. Keep it empty to leave ChatGPT without memory of previous messages.

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response
  Default value: `[`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "azure-openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask_gpt",
    "input": {
      "deploymentId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "temperature": 0.9,
      "maxTokens": 2048,
      "topP": 1,
      "frequencyPenalty": 0,
      "presencePenalty": 0.6,
      "memoryKey": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "roles": "["
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### List Rows

If provided rows will be order by specific field.Use **-** sign for descending / **+** sing for ascending ordering. Example. "-My Field" will return rows in descending order based on "My Field" field.

#### Parameters
- **table_id**: `Number`
  Please enter the table ID where you want to get the rows from. You can find the ID by clicking on the three dots next to the table. It's the number between brackets.
  **Required**: Yes

- **limit**: `Number`
  The maximum number of rows to return.

- **search**: `Text`
  If provided only rows with cell data that matches the search query are going to be returned.

- **order_by**: `Text`
  If provided rows will be order by specific field.Use **-** sign for descending / **+** sing for ascending ordering. Example. "-My Field" will return rows in descending order based on "My Field" field.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "baserow",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "baserow_list_rows",
    "input": {
      "table_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "limit": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "search": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "order_by": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Beamer Post

#### Parameters

  Enter the Title of the post
  Default value: `'Post`

  Enter the description of the post
  Default value: `'desc...'`
  **Required**: Yes

  Set Category
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | New | 'new' |
  | Fix | 'fix' |
  | Coming Soon | 'coming_soon' |
  | Announcement | 'announcement' |
  | Improvement | 'improvement' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **showInWidget**: `StaticDropdown`
  Check to enable widget
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | True | true |
  | False | false |

- **showInStandalone**: `StaticDropdown`
  Check to enable Standalone
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | True | true |
  | False | false |

- **enableFeedback**: `Boolean`
  Check to enable feedback
  Default value: `False`

- **enableReactions**: `Boolean`
  Check to enable feedback
  Default value: `False`

- **enableSocialShare**: `Boolean`
  Check to enable social share
  Default value: `False`

- **autoOpen**: `Boolean`
  Check to enable auto open
  Default value: `False`

- **sendPushNotification**: `Boolean`
  Check to enable Push Notifications
  Default value: `False`

- **userEmail**: `Text`
  Enter user email
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example

```json
  "settings": {

      "title": "'Post",
      "description": "'desc...'",
      "category": "'new'",
      "showInWidget": "true",
      "showInStandalone": "true",
      "enableFeedback": false,
      "enableReactions": false,
      "enableSocialShare": false,
      "autoOpen": false,
      "sendPushNotification": false,
      "userEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

```json
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

### Get Products

Get a list of products from Cartloom

---


### Create Discount

Create a discount in Cartloom

#### Parameters
- **title**: `Text`
  Enter the title of the discount
  **Required**: Yes

- **enabled**: `Boolean`
  Is this discount enabled?
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **auto**: `Boolean`
  Is this discount automatically applied?
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **unlimited**: `Boolean`
  Is this discount unlimited?
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **selfDestruct**: `Boolean`
  Remove the discount after use
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **applyOnce**: `Boolean`
  Apply the discount once per order
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select the type of discount
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Fixed Amount | 'fixed' |
  | Percentage | 'percent' |
  Default value: `'fixed'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **amount**: `Number`
  Enter the amount of the discount
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **target**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select the target of the discount
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Selected Products | 'product' |
  | Total | 'total' |
  | All Products | 'all' |
  Default value: `'all'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **startDate**: `DateTime`
  The start date of the discount. YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS
  **Required**: Yes

- **stopDate**: `DateTime`
  The stop date of the discount. YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS
  **Required**: Yes

- **optional**: `MarkDown`

- **code**: `Text`
  Enter the discount code. Leave blank for no code.

- **targetPids**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  Select the products to apply the discount to

- **targetAmount**: `Number`
  The target amount for the discount when the target is set to Total

- **targetQuantity**: `Number`
  The target quantity for the discount when the target is set to All or Products
  Default value: `0`

- **allowance**: `Number`
  The number of times the discount can be used

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "cartloom",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_discount",
    "input": {
      "title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "enabled": false,
      "auto": false,
      "unlimited": false,
      "selfDestruct": false,
      "applyOnce": false,
      "type": "'fixed'",
      "amount": 0,
      "target": "'product'",
      "startDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stopDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "optional": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "code": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "targetPids": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "targetAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "targetQuantity": 0,
      "allowance": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# ChargeKeep

Easy-to-use recurring and one-time payments software for Stripe & PayPal

## Actions

### Create Invoice

Creates a new invoice in the CRM.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  External Contact Reference (ID) . Will be used for looking a client

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Draft | 'Draft' |
  | Final | 'Final' |
  | Paid | 'Paid' |
  | Sent | 'Sent' |
  Default value: `'Draft'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceNo**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **date**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  **Required**: Yes

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **grandTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **discountTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **shippingTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **taxTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **bCompany**: `Text`

- **bFirstName**: `Text`

- **bLastName**: `Text`

- **bPhone**: `Text`

- **bEmail**: `Text`

- **bCountryId**: `Text`

- **bStateId**: `Text`

- **bStateName**: `Text`

- **bCity**: `Text`

- **bZip**: `Text`

- **bAddress1**: `Text`

- **bAddress2**: `Text`

- **sCompany**: `Text`

- **sFirstName**: `Text`

- **sLastName**: `Text`

- **sPhone**: `Text`

- **sEmail**: `Text`

- **sCountryId**: `Text`

- **sStateId**: `Text`

- **sStateName**: `Text`

- **sCity**: `Text`

- **sZip**: `Text`

- **sAddress1**: `Text`

- **sAddress2**: `Text`

- **note**: `Text`

- **invoiceDescription**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quantity**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **rate**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **itemTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **commissionableAmount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **unitId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Unit'`

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code. We will look up the product

- **itemDescription**: `Text`

- **sortOrder**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **transactionDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **transactionDescription**: `Text`

- **amount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **gatewayName**: `Text`

- **gatewayTransactionId**: `Text`

- **historicalData**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass true if this is not actual transaction. Should be False by default
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | true | true |
  | false | false |
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json

  "settings": {

      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

      "grandTotal": 0,
      "discountTotal": 0,
      "shippingTotal": 0,
      "taxTotal": 0,
      "bCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

      "bLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bZip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sFirstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

### Add or Update Contact

The contact's full name.

#### Parameters
- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **fullName**: `Text`
  The contact's full name.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **industry**: `Text`
  The company's industry.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work/primary phone number.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's mobile phone number.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **addressLine2**: `Text`

- **city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "chargekeep",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateContact",
    "input": {
      "importType": "'Lead'",
      "matchExisting": "true",
      "contactId": 0,
      "fullName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "namePrefix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "middleName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nickName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nameSuffix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gender": "'Male'",
      "dob": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bankCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ssn": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "companyName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "jobTitle": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "industry": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workEmail1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workPhone1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "homePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "mobilePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "webSiteUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedInUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "photoUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "street": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "addressLine2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "city": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "zip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "experience": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "profileSummary": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "followUpDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "assignedUser": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadDealAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadSource": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "channelId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "affiliateCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "refererURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "entryUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Product

Creates a new product in the CRM

#### Parameters
- **productType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | General | 'General' |
  | Event | 'Event' |
  | Subscription | 'Subscription' |
  | Digital | 'Digital' |
  Default value: `'General'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **code**: `Text`
  Sku is the product code
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **descriptionHTML**: `Text`
  Javascript and media tags are not allowed

- **logoURL**: `Text`

- **groupName**: `Text`

- **price**: `Number`
  Required for General , Digital and Event Product Type
  Default value: `0`

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`

- **unit**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Day'`

- **frequency**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  | OneTime | 'OneTime' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`

- **fee**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **cycles**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **signupFee**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **customPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Days | 'Days' |
  | Weeks | 'Weeks' |
  | Months | 'Months' |
  | Years | 'Years' |
  Default value: `'Days'`

- **customPeriodCount**: `Number`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Default value: `0`

- **trialDayCount**: `Number`
  Required for OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **gracePeriodDayCount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "chargekeep",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createProduct",
    "input": {
      "productType": "'General'",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "code": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "descriptionHTML": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "logoURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "groupName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "price": 0,
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "unit": "'Day'",
      "frequency": "'Monthly'",
      "fee": 0,
      "cycles": 0,
      "signupFee": 0,
      "customPeriodType": "'Days'",
      "customPeriodCount": 0,
      "trialDayCount": 0,
      "gracePeriodDayCount": 0
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Add or Update Contact (Extended

The contact's middle name.

#### Parameters
- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **overrideLists**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will override lists of contact details in update mode instead of merging them - lists, tags, emails, phones, links, addresses, photos.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

- **ignoreInvalidValues**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will save the record even if there are some validation errors.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  This is string external reference that can be passed during creation and then if sent again it will update the record.

- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **createUser**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then User will be created. Personal email will be used as User Name.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **sendWelcomeEmail**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then Welcome Email will be sent to the newly created user.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **userPassword**: `Text`
  If password is not passed then it will be automatically generated.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **drivingLicense**: `Text`

- **drivingLicenseState**: `Text`

- **isActiveMilitaryDuty**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **isUSCitizen**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **preferredToD**: `StaticDropdown`
  Preferred Time of Day to contact with Client
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Morning | 'Morning' |
  | Afternoon | 'Afternoon' |
  | Evening | 'Evening' |
  | Anytime | 'Anytime' |

- **personAffiliateCode**: `Text`
  Affiliate Code is used for the current person detection as a source of new leads. Alphanumeric characters, underscore and hyphen are allowed.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative personal email.

- **email3**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

  The contact's home phone number.

- **homePhoneExt**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number extension.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work phone number.

  The contact's work phone number extension.

- **workPhone2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number.

- **workPhone2Ext**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number extension.

- **home_street**: `Text`

- **home_countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

### Add or Update Subscription

Creates a new subscription.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **productId**: `Number`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  ContactXref have to be specified and correct to look up the correct contact

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code (Unique product identifier). ProductCode have to be specified and correct to look up the correct product
  **Required**: Yes

- **paymentPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **hasRecurringBilling**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "chargekeep",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateSubscription",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "productId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "paymentPeriodType": "'Monthly'",
      "hasRecurringBilling": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Anthropic Claude
## Actions

### Extract Structured Data

The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Parameters
- **model**: `StaticDropdown`
  The model which will generate the completion. Some models are suitable for natural language tasks, others specialize in code.
  Default value: `'claude-3-haiku-20240307'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **text**: `Text`
  Text to extract structured data from.

- **image**: `File`
  Image or PDF to extract structured data from.

- **prompt**: `Text`
  Prompt to guide the AI.
  Default value: `'Extract`

- **schema**: `DynamicProperties`
  **Required**: Yes

- **fields**: `JSON`
  Learn more about JSON Schema here: https://json-schema.org/learn/getting-started-step-by-step
  Default value: `{`
  **Required**: Yes

- **fields**: `Array`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  Provide the name of the value you want to extract from the unstructured text. The name should be unique and short.
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`
  Brief description of the data, this hints for the AI on what to look for

- **type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Type of parameter.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Text | 'string' |
  | Number | 'number' |
  | Boolean | 'boolean' |
  Default value: `'string'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **isRequired**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "anthropic-claude",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "extract-structured-data",
    "input": {
      "model": "'claude-3-haiku-20240307'",
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "prompt": "'Extract",
      "schema": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "fields": "{",
      "fields": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "type": "'string'",
      "isRequired": false,
      "maxTokens": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Ask Claude

Array of roles to specify more accurate response.Please check [guide to Input Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages-examples#vision).

#### Parameters
- **model**: `StaticDropdown`
  The model which will generate the completion. Some models are suitable for natural language tasks, others specialize in code.
  Default value: `'claude-3-haiku-20240307'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **systemPrompt**: `Text`
  Default value: `"You're`

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

- **prompt**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **image**: `File`
  URL of image to be used as input for the model.

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response.Please check [guide to Input Messages](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/api/messages-examples#vision).

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "anthropic-claude",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask_claude",
    "input": {
      "model": "'claude-3-haiku-20240307'",
      "systemPrompt": "\"You're",
      "temperature": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "maxTokens": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "roles": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### Get Entries

Fetches entries from clockodo

#### Parameters
- **time_since**: `DateTime`
  **Required**: Yes

- **time_until**: `DateTime`
  **Required**: Yes

- **user_id_filter**: `Number`
  Filter entries by their user

- **customer_id_filter**: `Number`
  Filter entries by their customer

- **project_id_filter**: `Number`
  Filter entries by their project

- **service_id_filter**: `Number`
  Filter entries by their service

- **billable_filter**: `Boolean`
  Only show entries that are billable

- **billed_filter**: `Boolean`
  Only show entries that are already billed

- **enhanced_list**: `Boolean`
  Retrieves additional information about the entries

- **page**: `Number`
  Reads only the specified page

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {

    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "list_entries",
    "input": {
      "time_since": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "time_until": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "user_id_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "customer_id_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "project_id_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "service_id_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "billable_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "billed_filter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "enhanced_list": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Crypto

Generate random passwords and hash existing text

## Actions

### Generate Password

Generates a random password with the specified length

#### Parameters
- **length**: `Number`
  The length of the password (maximum 256
  **Required**: Yes

- **characterSet**: `StaticDropdown`
  The character set to use when generating the password
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Alphanumeric | 'alphanumeric' |
  | Alphanumeric + Symbols | 'alphanumeric-symbols' |
  Default value: `'alphanumeric'`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "crypto",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "generate-password",
    "input": {
      "length": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "characterSet": "'alphanumeric'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Generate HMAC Signature

Converts text to a HMAC signed hash value using various hashing algorithms

#### Parameters
- **secretKey**: `Text`
  The secret key to encrypt
  **Required**: Yes

- **method**: `StaticDropdown`
  The hashing algorithm to use
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | MD5 | 'md5' |
  | SHA256 | 'sha256' |
  | SHA512 | 'sha512' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **text**: `Text`
  The text to be hashed and encrypted
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "crypto",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "hmac-signature",
    "input": {
      "secretKey": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "method": "'md5'",
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

Converts text to a hash value using various hashing algorithms

#### Parameters
- **method**: `StaticDropdown`
  The hashing algorithm to use
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | MD5 | 'md5' |
  | SHA256 | 'sha256' |
  | SHA512 | 'sha512' |
  | SHA3-512 | 'sha3-512' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **text**: `Text`
  The text to be hashed
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "crypto",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "hash-text",
    "input": {
      "method": "'md5'",
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {

    }
  }
```

# CSV

Manipulate CSV text

## Actions

### Convert CSV to JSON

This function reads a CSV string and converts it into JSON array format.

#### Parameters
- **csv_text**: `Text`
  Default value: `''`
  **Required**: Yes

- **has_headers**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **delimiter_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select the delimiter type for the CSV text.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Comma | ' |
  | Tab | '\t' |
  Default value: `''`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "csv",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "convert_csv_to_json",
    "input": {
      "csv_text": "''",
      "has_headers": false,
      "delimiter_type": "'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Comma | ' |
  | Tab | '\t' |
  Default value: `'`
  **Required**: Yes

```json
{
  "valid": true,
```

# Date Helper

### Add/Subtract Time

Provide an expression to add or subtract using the following units (year , month , day , hour , minute or second). Examples: + 2 second + 1 hour + 1 year - 3 day - 2 month + 5 minute

#### Parameters
- **inputDate**: `Text`
  Enter the input date
  **Required**: Yes

- **inputDateFormat**: `StaticDropdown`
  Default value: `getCorrectedFormat(timeFormat.format00)`
  **Required**: Yes

- **outputFormat**: `StaticDropdown`
  Default value: `getCorrectedFormat(timeFormat.format00)`
  **Required**: Yes

- **expression**: `Text`
  Provide an expression to add or subtract using the following units (year , month , day , hour , minute or second). Examples: + 2 second + 1 hour + 1 year - 3 day - 2 month + 5 minute
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "date-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "add_subtract_date",
    "input": {
      "inputDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "inputDateFormat": "getCorrectedFormat(timeFormat.format00)",
      "outputFormat": "getCorrectedFormat(timeFormat.format00)",
      "expression": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Date Difference

  **Required**: Yes

  **Required**: Yes

  **Required**: Yes

  **Required**: Yes

- **unitDifference**: `StaticMultiSelectDropdown`
  Select the unit of difference between the two dates
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|

  | Month | timeParts.month |
  | Day | timeParts.day |
  | Hour | timeParts.hour |

```json
      "startDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "startDateFormat": "timeFormat.format00",

    },

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

  Available options:

  |-------|-------|

  | Month | timeParts.month |
  | Day | timeParts.day |
  | Hour | timeParts.hour |
  | Minute | timeParts.minute |
  | Second | timeParts.second |
  | Day of Week | timeParts.dayOfWeek |

```json
    "input": {

    "inputUiInfo": {},

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Next Day of Year

Get the date and time of the next day of the year

#### Parameters
- **month**: `StaticDropdown`
  The month that you would like to get the date and time of.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | January | 1 |
  | February | 2 |
  | March | 3 |
  | April | 4 |
  | May | 5 |
  | June | 6 |
  | July | 7 |
  | August | 8 |
  | September | 9 |
  | October | 10 |
  | November | 11 |
  | December | 12 |
  **Required**: Yes

- **day**: `Number`
  The day of the month that you would like to get the date and time of.
  Default value: `1`
  **Required**: Yes

- **time**: `Text`
  The time that you would like to get the date and time of. This must be in 24h format.
  Default value: `'00:00'`

- **currentTime**: `Boolean`
  If checked, the current time will be used instead of the time specified above.
  Default value: `False`

- **timeFormat**: `StaticDropdown`
  Default value: `timeFormat.format00`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "date-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "next_day_of_year",
    "input": {
      "month": "1",
      "day": 1,
      "time": "'00:00'",
      "currentTime": false,
      "timeFormat": "timeFormat.format00"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# DeepL

AI-powered language translation

## Actions

### Translate text

The automatic detection of the XML structure won't yield best results in all XML files.

#### Parameters
- **text**: `Text`
  Text to be translated. Only UTF-8-encoded plain text is supported.
  **Required**: Yes

- **target_lang**: `StaticDropdown`
  The language into which the text should be translated.
  **Required**: Yes

- **source_lang**: `StaticDropdown`
  Language of the text to be translated

- **split_sentences**: `StaticDropdown`
  Sets whether the translation engine should first split the input into sentences. For text translations where tag_handling is not set to html, the default value is 1, meaning the engine splits on punctuation and on newlines.

- **preserve_formatting**: `StaticDropdown`
  Sets whether the translation engine should respect the original formatting, even if it would usually correct some aspects.

- **formality**: `StaticDropdown`
  Sets whether the translated text should lean towards formal or informal language.

- **glossary_id**: `Text`
  Specify the glossary to use for the translation.

- **tag_handling**: `StaticDropdown`
  Sets which kind of tags should be handled.

- **outline_detection**: `StaticDropdown`
  The automatic detection of the XML structure won't yield best results in all XML files.

- **non_splitting_tags**: `Text`
  Comma-separated list of XML or HTML tags.

- **splitting_tags**: `Text`
  Comma-separated list of XML or HTML tags.

- **ignore_tags**: `Text`
  Comma-separated list of XML or HTML tags.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "deepl",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "translate_text",
    "input": {
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "target_lang": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "source_lang": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "split_sentences": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "preserve_formatting": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "formality": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "glossary_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tag_handling": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

      "splitting_tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ignore_tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Delay

Use it to delay the execution of the next action

## Actions

### Delay For

Delays the execution of the next action for a given duration

#### Parameters
- **markdown**: `MarkDown`

- **unit**: `StaticDropdown`
  The unit of time to delay the execution of the next action
  Default value: `TimeUnit.SECONDS`
  **Required**: Yes

- **delayFor**: `Number`
  The number of units to delay the execution of the next action
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "delay",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "delayFor",
    "input": {
      "markdown": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "unit": "TimeUnit.SECONDS",
      "delayFor": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Delay Until

Delays the execution of the next action until a given timestamp

#### Parameters
- **markdown**: `MarkDown`

- **delayUntilTimestamp**: `DateTime`
  Specifies the date and time until which the execution of the next action should be delayed. It supports multiple formats, including ISO format.
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "delay",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "delay_until",
    "input": {
      "markdown": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "delayUntilTimestamp": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Dropbox

Cloud storage and file synchronization

## Actions

### Copy folder

If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the folder to avoid conflict.

#### Parameters
- **from_path**: `Text`
  The source path of the folder (e.g. /folder1/sourceFolder
  **Required**: Yes

- **to_path**: `Text`
  The destination path for the copied folder (e.g. /folder2/destinationFolder
  **Required**: Yes

- **autorename**: `Boolean`
  If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the folder to avoid conflict.
  Default value: `False`

- **allow_ownership_transfer**: `Boolean`
  Allows copy by owner even if it would result in an ownership transfer.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "copy_dropbox_folder",
    "input": {
      "from_path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "to_path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "autorename": false,
      "allow_ownership_transfer": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Create New Folder

If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the folder to avoid the conflict. The default for this field is False.

#### Parameters
- **path**: `Text`
  The path of the new folder e.g. /Homework/math
  **Required**: Yes

- **autorename**: `Boolean`
  If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the folder to avoid the conflict. The default for this field is False.

#### Example

```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_new_dropbox_folder",

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Move file

If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the file to avoid conflict.

#### Parameters
- **from_path**: `Text`
  The current path of the file (e.g. /folder1/oldfile.txt
  **Required**: Yes

- **to_path**: `Text`
  The new path for the file (e.g. /folder2/newfile.txt
  **Required**: Yes

- **autorename**: `Boolean`
  If there's a conflict, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the file to avoid conflict.
  Default value: `False`

- **allow_ownership_transfer**: `Boolean`
  Allows moves by owner even if it would result in an ownership transfer.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "move_dropbox_file",
    "input": {
      "from_path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "to_path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "autorename": false,
      "allow_ownership_transfer": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Upload file

If there's a conflict, as determined by mode, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the file to avoid conflict.

#### Parameters
- **path**: `Text`
  The path where the file should be saved (e.g. /folder1/file.txt
  **Required**: Yes

- **file**: `File`
  The file URL or base64 to upload
  **Required**: Yes

- **autorename**: `Boolean`
  If there's a conflict, as determined by mode, have the Dropbox server try to autorename the file to avoid conflict.
  Default value: `False`

- **mute**: `Boolean`
  Normally, users are made aware of any file modifications in their Dropbox account via notifications in the client software. If true, this tells the clients that this modification shouldn't result in a user notification.

- **strict_conflict**: `Boolean`
  Be more strict about how each WriteMode detects conflict. For example, always return a conflict error when mode = WriteMode.update and the given "rev" doesn't match the existing file's "rev", even if the existing file has been deleted.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "upload_dropbox_file",
    "input": {
      "path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "file": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "autorename": false,
      "mute": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "strict_conflict": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### List a folder

List the contents of a folder

#### Parameters
- **path**: `Text`
  The path of the folder to be listed (e.g. /folder1). Use an empty string for the root folder.
  **Required**: Yes

- **recursive**: `Boolean`
  If set to true, the list folder operation will be applied recursively to all subfolders and the response will contain contents of all subfolders.
  Default value: `False`

- **limit**: `Number`
  The maximum number of results to return (between 1 and 2000). Default is 2000 if not specified.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "list_dropbox_folder",
    "input": {
      "path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recursive": false,
      "limit": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Search

Search for files and folders

#### Parameters
- **query**: `Text`
  The search string. Must be at least 3 characters.
  **Required**: Yes

- **path**: `Text`
  The path to search in. If not specified, the search is performed from the root.

- **max_results**: `Number`
  The maximum number of search results to return (up to 1000). Default is 100 if not specified.

- **order_by**: `StaticDropdown`
  Specified property of the order of search results.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Relevance | 'relevance' |
  | Modified Time | 'modified_time' |
  Default value: `'relevance'`

- **file_status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Restricts search to the given file status.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Active | 'active' |
  | Deleted | 'deleted' |
  Default value: `'active'`

- **filename_only**: `Boolean`
  Restricts search to only match on filenames.
  Default value: `False`

- **file_extensions**: `Text`
  Restricts search to only the extensions specified (comma-separated).

- **file_categories**: `Text`
  Restricts search to only the file categories specified (comma-separated).

- **account_id**: `Text`
  Restricts results to the given account id.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "dropbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "search_dropbox",
    "input": {
      "query": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "path": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "max_results": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "order_by": "'relevance'",
      "file_status": "'active'",
      "filename_only": false,
      "file_extensions": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "file_categories": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "account_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Freshdesk

Customer support software

## Actions

### Get Tickets

Get Ticket instances from Freshdesk.

---


### Get Freshdesk Contacts

Get contact details from Freshdesk for all (optional filtered) contacts.

#### Parameters
- **filter_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select one and provide the value.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | E-mail | 'email' |
  | Mobile | 'mobile' |
  | Phone | 'phone' |
  | Company ID | 'company_id' |
  | Updated Since | 'updated_since' |
  Default value: `''`

- **filter_value**: `Text`
  Provide value if previous option selected!
  Default value: `''`

- **filter_status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Can filter by state: blocked, deleted, unverified or verified.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Blocked | 'blocked' |
  | Deleted | 'deleted' |
  | Unverified | 'unverified' |
  | Verified | 'verified' |
  Default value: `''`

- **per_page**: `Number`
  Freshdesk calls this per_page - set to 0 for all, if specified maximum is 100
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "freshdesk",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_contacts",
    "input": {
      "filter_type": "'email'",
      "filter_value": "''",
      "filter_status": "'blocked'",
      "per_page": 0
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Freshsales

Sales CRM software

## Actions

### Create Contact

Add new contact in Freshsales CRM

#### Parameters
- **first_name**: `Text`
  First name of the contact

- **last_name**: `Text`
  Last name of the contact

- **job_title**: `Text`
  Designation of the contact in the account they belong to

- **email**: `Text`
  Primary email address of the contact
  **Required**: Yes

- **work_number**: `Text`
  Work phone number of the contact

- **mobile_number**: `Text`
  Mobile phone number of the contact

- **address**: `Text`
  Address of the contact

- **city**: `Text`
  City that the contact belongs to

- **state**: `Text`
  State that the contact belongs to

- **zipcode**: `Text`
  Zipcode of the region that the contact belongs to

- **country**: `Text`
  Country that the contact belongs to

- **territory_id**: `Text`
  ID of the territory that the contact belongs to

- **owner_id**: `Text`
  ID of the user to whom the contact has been assigned

- **subscription_status**: `Text`
  Status of subscription that the contact is in.

- **medium**: `Text`
  The medium that led your contact to your website/web app

- **campaign_id**: `Text`
  The campaign that led your contact to your web app.

- **keyword**: `Text`
  The keywords that the contact used to reach your website/web app

- **time_zone**: `Text`
  Timezone that the contact belongs to

- **facebook**: `Text`
  Facebook username of the contact

- **twitter**: `Text`
  Twitter username of the contact

- **linkedin**: `Text`
  LinkedIn account of the contact

- **contact_status_id**: `Text`
  ID of the contact status that the contact belongs to

- **sales_account_id**: `Text`
  ID of the primary account that the contact belongs to

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "freshsales",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "freshsales_create_contact",
    "input": {
      "first_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "last_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "job_title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "work_number": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "mobile_number": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "address": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "city": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "state": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "zipcode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "country": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "territory_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "owner_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "subscription_status": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "medium": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "campaign_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "keyword": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "time_zone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "facebook": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "twitter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedin": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "contact_status_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sales_account_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
```

### Send Email

The address must be listed in your GMail account's settings

#### Parameters
- **receiver**: `Array`
  **Required**: Yes

- **cc**: `Array`

- **bcc**: `Array`

- **subject**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **body_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | plain text | 'plain_text' |
  | html | 'html' |
  Default value: `'plain_text'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **body**: `Text`
  Body for the email you want to send
  **Required**: Yes

- **reply_to**: `Array`
  Email address to set as the "Reply-To" header

- **sender_name**: `Text`

- **from**: `Text`
  The address must be listed in your GMail account's settings

- **attachment**: `File`
  File to attach to the email you want to send

- **attachment_name**: `Text`
  In case you want to change the name of the attachment

- **in_reply_to**: `Text`
  Reply to this Message-ID

- **draft**: `Boolean`
  Create draft without sending the actual email
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "gmail",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send_email",
    "input": {
      "receiver": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cc": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bcc": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "subject": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "body_type": "'plain_text'",
      "body": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "reply_to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sender_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "from": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "attachment": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "attachment_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "in_reply_to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "draft": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

## Triggers

### New Labeled Email

Triggers when a label is added to an email

---


### New Email

Triggers when new mail is found in your Gmail inbox

---

```json
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_document_based_on_template",
    "input": {
      "template": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

    "inputUiInfo": {},
```

```json
    "actionName": "chat_gemini",
    "input": {
      "model": "defaultLLM",
```
