# Harvest

Time Tracking Software with Invoicing

## Actions

### Get Users

Fetches Users

#### Parameters
- **is_active**: `Text`
  Pass `true` to only return active users and `false` to return inactive users.

- **updated_since**: `Text`
  Only return users that have been updated since the given date and time.

- **page**: `Text`
  DEPRECATED: The page number to use in pagination.

- **per_page**: `Text`
  The number of records to return per page. (1-2000

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "harvest",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_users",
    "input": {
      "is_active": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "updated_since": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "per_page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Uninvoiced Report

Uninvoiced hours and expenses for all billable projects

#### Parameters
- **from**: `Text`
  Only report on time entries and expenses with a spent_date on or after the given date. (YYYY-MM-DD
  **Required**: Yes

- **to**: `Text`
  Only report on time entries and expenses with a spent_date on or before the given date. (YYYY-MM-DD
  **Required**: Yes

- **include_fixed_fee**: `Text`
  Whether or not to include fixed-fee projects in the response. (Default: true

- **page**: `Text`
  The page number to use in pagination.

- **per_page**: `Text`
  The number of records to return per page. (1-2000

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "harvest",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "reports-uninvoiced",
    "input": {
      "from": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "include_fixed_fee": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "per_page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Get Clients

Fetches Clients

#### Parameters
- **is_active**: `Text`
  Pass `true` to only return active clients and `false` to return inactive clients.

- **updated_since**: `Text`
  Only return clients that have been updated since the given date and time.

- **page**: `Text`
  DEPRECATED: The page number to use in pagination.

- **per_page**: `Text`
  The number of records to return per page. (1-2000

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "harvest",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_clients",
    "input": {
      "is_active": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "updated_since": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "per_page": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---




# Heartbeat

Monitoring and alerting made easy

## Actions

### Create User

The user's full name

#### Parameters
- **name**: `Text`
  The user's full name
  **Required**: Yes

- **email**: `Text`
  The user's email. Must be unique to the community
  **Required**: Yes

- **role_id**: `Dropdown`
  The role the user should have
  **Required**: Yes

- **group_ids**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  A list of the ids of the groups that the user should belong to.

- **profile_picture**: `Text`
  A Data URI scheme in the JPG, GIF, or PNG format. Ensure you use the proper content type (image/jpeg, image/png, image/gif) that matches the image data being provided

- **bio**: `Text`
  The user's bio

- **status**: `Text`
  The user's status

- **linkedin**: `Text`
  A link to the user's LinkedIn profile

- **twitter**: `Text`
  A link to the user's Twitter profile

- **instagram**: `Text`
  A link to the user's Instagram profile

- **create_introduction_thread**: `Boolean`
  If true and a value for bio is provided, an introduction thread for the user will be created in the channel designated for introductions in your community settings.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "heartbeat",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "heartbeat_create_user",
    "input": {
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "role_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "group_ids": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "profile_picture": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bio": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedin": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "twitter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "instagram": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "create_introduction_thread": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

- **eventType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Sent | 'SENT' |
  | Dropped | 'DROPPED' |
  | Processed | 'PROCESSED' |
  | Delivered | 'DELIVERED' |
  | Deferred | 'DEFERRED' |
  | Bounce | 'BOUNCE' |
  | Open | 'OPEN' |
  | Click | 'CLICK' |
  | Status Change | 'STATUSCHANGE' |
  | Spam Report | 'SPAMREPORT' |

#### Example
```json
{
  "trigger": {
    "valid": true,
    "type": "POLLING",
    "settings": {
      "eventType": "'SENT'"
    }
  }
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

# Image Helper

Tools for image manipulations

## Actions

### Rotate an image

Rotates an image

#### Parameters
- **image**: `File`
  **Required**: Yes

- **degree**: `StaticDropdown`
  Specifies the degree of clockwise rotation applied to the image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **resultFileName**: `Text`
  Specifies the output file name for the result image (without extension).

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "image-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "rotate_image",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "degree": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "resultFileName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

  **Required**: Yes

- **width**: `Number`
  Specifies the width of the image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **height**: `Number`
  Specifies the height of the image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **aspectRatio**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

- **resultFileName**: `Text`
  Specifies the output file name for the result image (without extension).

#### Example

```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "image-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "resize_image",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "width": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "height": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "aspectRatio": false,
      "resultFileName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Image to Base64

Converts an image to an url-like Base64 string

#### Parameters
- **image**: `File`
  The image to convert
  **Required**: Yes

- **override_mime_type**: `Text`
  The mime type to use when converting the image. In case you want to override the default mime type. Example image/png

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "image-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "image_to_base64",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "override_mime_type": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Compresses an image

Compresses an image

#### Parameters
- **image**: `File`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quality**: `StaticDropdown`
  Specifies the quality of the image after compression (0-100).
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | High Quality | 90 |
  | Lossy Quality | 60 |
  **Required**: Yes

- **format**: `StaticDropdown`
  Specifies the format of the image after compression.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | JPG | 'jpg' |
  | PNG | 'png' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **resultFileName**: `Text`
  Specifies the output file name for the result image (without extension).

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "image-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "compress_image",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "quality": "90",
      "format": "'jpg'",
      "resultFileName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Crop an image

Crops an image

#### Parameters
- **image**: `File`
  **Required**: Yes

- **left**: `Number`
  Specifies the horizontal position, indicating where the cropping starts from the left side of the image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **top**: `Number`
  Represents the vertical position, indicating the starting point from the top of the image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **width**: `Number`
  Determines the horizontal size of the cropped area.
  **Required**: Yes

- **height**: `Number`
  Determines the vertical size of the cropped area.
  **Required**: Yes

- **resultFileName**: `Text`
  Specifies the output file name for the cropped image (without extension).

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "image-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "crop_image",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "left": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "top": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "width": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "height": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "resultFileName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Instasent
## Actions

### Add Event

${param.description} (Max ${param.multiValue} values

#### Parameters
- **user_id**: `Text`
  Unique identifier of the user
  **Required**: Yes

- **event_id**: `Text`
  Unique identifier for this event. Used for deduplication.
  **Required**: Yes

- **event_date**: `Text`
  Date and time when the event occurred, will default to now (ISO 8601 format YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS.SSSZ

- **event_type**: `Dropdown`
  Select the type of event to create
  **Required**: Yes

- **event_parameters**: `DynamicProperties`
  ${param.description} (Max ${param.multiValue} values
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "instasent",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "add_event",
    "input": {
      "user_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_date": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_type": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_parameters": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Add/Update contact

${description} (Max ${spec.multivalue} values

#### Parameters
- **contact**: `DynamicProperties`
  ${description} (Max ${spec.multivalue} values
  **Required**: Yes

- **instant**: `Boolean`
  Process contact immediately instead of queuing. Only enable this when you need to add an event for this contact in the next step. Not recommended for high-volume operations.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "instasent",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "add_or_update_contact",
    "input": {
      "contact": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "instant": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Intercom

Customer messaging platform for sales, marketing, and support

## Actions

### Find Conversation

Searches for conversations using various criteria

#### Parameters
- **searchField**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Conversation ID | 'id' |
  | Subject | 'source.subject' |
  | Message Body | 'source.body' |
  | Author Email | 'source.author.email' |
  | Assigned Admin | 'admin_assignee_id' |
  | Team | 'team_assignee_id' |
  | Tag IDs | 'tag_ids' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **matchType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Contains | 'contains' |
  | Equals | 'equals' |
  | Starts With | 'starts_with' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **searchTerm**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Open | 'open' |
  | Closed | 'closed' |

- **updateAfter**: `DateTime`

- **updateBefore**: `DateTime`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "intercom",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "find-conversation",
    "input": {
      "searchField": "'id'",
      "matchType": "'contains'",
      "searchTerm": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "'open'",
      "updateAfter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "updateBefore": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Get or Create Contact

Get or create a contact (ie. user or lead) if it isn't found

#### Parameters
- **role**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | User | ContactRole.USER |
  | Lead | ContactRole.LEAD |
  Default value: `ContactRole.USER`
  **Required**: Yes

- **email**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **external_id**: `Text`

- **name**: `Text`

- **phone**: `Text`

- **avatar**: `Text`
  An image URL containing the avatar of a contact

- **custom_attributes**: `Object`

```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "intercom",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_or_create_contact",
    "input": {
      "role": "ContactRole.USER",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

      "avatar": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

### Send Message

Send a message to a contact (only allowed by admins

  Default value: `MessageType.EMAIL`
  **Required**: Yes

- **email_required_fields**: `DynamicProperties`
  **Required**: Yes

- **subject**: `Text`
  Email title
  **Required**: Yes

- **template**: `StaticDropdown`
  Style of the email
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Personal | 'personal' |
  | Plain | 'plain' |
  Default value: `'personal'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **body**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **create_conversation_without_contact_reply**: `Boolean`
  Whether a conversation should be opened in the inbox for the message without the contact replying. Defaults to false if not provided.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "intercom",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send_message",
    "input": {
      "message_type": "MessageType.EMAIL",
      "email_required_fields": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "subject": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "template": "'personal'",
      "body": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "create_conversation_without_contact_reply": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,

    }
  }
}
```

# Invoice Ninja

Free open-source invoicing tool

## Actions

### Create Invoice

Creates an invoice in Invoice Ninja for billing purposes.

#### Parameters
- **client_id**: `Text`
  Client ID from Invoice Ninja
  **Required**: Yes

- **purchase_order_no**: `Text`
  Descriptive text or arbitrary number (optional

- **discount**: `Text`
  Enter a number for the whole invoice discount
  Default value: `'0'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **discount_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select either amount or percentage for invoice discount. Applies to line items and invoice.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Amount | true |
  | Percentage | false |
  Default value: `True`
  **Required**: Yes

- **public_notes**: `Text`
  Text that may be visible in the client portal (optional

- **private_notes**: `Text`
  Text not visible for clients (optional

- **order_items_json**: `Text`
  e.g., [{ "quantity":1,"product_key":"product key", "discount": "0" }]
  **Required**: Yes

- **send_email**: `Boolean`
  Should we send the invoice to the client on creation?
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **mark_sent**: `Boolean`
  Makes the invoice active otherwise remains pending.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **due_date**: `DateTime`
  e.g., 2024-01-20

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "invoice-ninja",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_invoice",
    "input": {
      "client_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "purchase_order_no": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "discount": "'0'",
      "discount_type": "true",
      "public_notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "private_notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "order_items_json": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "send_email": false,
      "mark_sent": false,
      "due_date": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Create Client

Creates a new client in InvoiceNinja.

#### Parameters
- **client_first_name**: `Text`
  The contact first name for this client (optional

- **client_last_name**: `Text`
  The contact last name for this client (optional

- **client_phone**: `Text`
  The contact number for this client (optional

- **client_email**: `Text`
  The contact email for this client (compulsory
  **Required**: Yes

- **client_send_email**: `Boolean`
  Should we send invoices to the client by e-mail?
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **client_business_name**: `Text`
  Name of this business or natural person (compulsory
  **Required**: Yes

- **client_tax_no**: `Text`
  Leave blank if not a business (optional

- **client_private_notes**: `Text`
  Text not visible for clients (optional

- **client_address1**: `Text`
  Usually street name and number (compulsory
  **Required**: Yes

- **client_address2**: `Text`
  Additional address details (optional

- **client_city**: `Text`
  City or Town name (compulsory
  **Required**: Yes

- **client_state**: `Text`
  State or county or similar (optional

- **client_postcode**: `Text`
  Postal code (optional

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "invoice-ninja",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_client",
    "input": {
      "client_first_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_last_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_phone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_send_email": false,
      "client_business_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_tax_no": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "client_private_notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

  **Required**: Yes

  | Stop | 'stop' |

  | Restore | 'restore' |

```json
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Event On Data

Handle EventOnData events via webhooks

#### Parameters
- **format**: `StaticDropdown`
  Select the output format
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Simple format | 'simple' |
  | Advanced format | 'advanced' |
  Default value: `'simple'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **event1**: `StaticDropdown`
  Which events will trigger this hook
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Data Deleted | 'delete' |
  | Data Saved | 'finished' |
  | Data Updated | 'update' |
  | Push Received | 'pull' |
  | Push Send | 'push' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **event2**: `StaticDropdown`
  Which events will trigger this hook
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  |  | '' |
  | Data Deleted | 'delete' |
  | Data Saved | 'finished' |
  | Data Updated | 'update' |
  | Push Received | 'pull' |
  | Push Send | 'push' |

- **event3**: `StaticDropdown`
  Which events will trigger this hook
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  |  | '' |
  | Data Deleted | 'delete' |
  | Data Saved | 'finished' |
  | Data Updated | 'update' |
  | Push Received | 'pull' |
  | Push Send | 'push' |

- **event4**: `StaticDropdown`
  Which events will trigger this hook
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  |  | '' |
  | Data Deleted | 'delete' |
  | Data Saved | 'finished' |
  | Data Updated | 'update' |
  | Push Received | 'pull' |
  | Push Send | 'push' |

- **event5**: `StaticDropdown`
  Which events will trigger this hook
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  |  | '' |
  | Data Deleted | 'delete' |
  | Data Saved | 'finished' |
  | Data Updated | 'update' |
  | Push Received | 'pull' |
  | Push Send | 'push' |

#### Example
```json
{
  "trigger": {
    "valid": true,
    "type": "WEBHOOK",
    "settings": {
      "format": "'simple'",
      "event1": "'delete'",
      "event2": "''",
      "event3": "''",
      "event4": "''",
      "event5": "''"
    }
  }
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

# Linka

Linka white-label B2B marketplace platform powers communities and digital storefronts

## Actions

### Add or Update Contact

The contact's full name.

#### Parameters
- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **fullName**: `Text`
  The contact's full name.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **industry**: `Text`
  The company's industry.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work/primary phone number.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's mobile phone number.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **addressLine2**: `Text`

- **city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "linka",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateContact",
    "input": {
      "importType": "'Lead'",
      "matchExisting": "true",
      "contactId": 0,
      "fullName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "namePrefix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "middleName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nickName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nameSuffix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gender": "'Male'",
      "dob": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bankCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ssn": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "companyName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "jobTitle": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "industry": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workEmail1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workPhone1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "homePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "mobilePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "webSiteUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedInUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "photoUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "street": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "addressLine2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "city": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "zip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "experience": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "profileSummary": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "followUpDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "assignedUser": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadDealAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadSource": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "channelId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "affiliateCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "refererURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "entryUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Invoice

Creates a new invoice in the CRM.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  External Contact Reference (ID) . Will be used for looking a client

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Draft | 'Draft' |
  | Final | 'Final' |
  | Paid | 'Paid' |
  | Sent | 'Sent' |
  Default value: `'Draft'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceNo**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **date**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  **Required**: Yes

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **grandTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **discountTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **shippingTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **taxTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **bCompany**: `Text`

- **bFirstName**: `Text`

- **bLastName**: `Text`

- **bPhone**: `Text`

- **bEmail**: `Text`

- **bCountryId**: `Text`

- **bStateId**: `Text`

- **bStateName**: `Text`

- **bCity**: `Text`

- **bZip**: `Text`

- **bAddress1**: `Text`

- **bAddress2**: `Text`

- **sCompany**: `Text`

- **sFirstName**: `Text`

- **sLastName**: `Text`

- **sPhone**: `Text`

- **sEmail**: `Text`

- **sCountryId**: `Text`

- **sStateId**: `Text`

- **sStateName**: `Text`

- **sCity**: `Text`

- **sZip**: `Text`

- **sAddress1**: `Text`

- **sAddress2**: `Text`

- **note**: `Text`

- **invoiceDescription**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quantity**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **rate**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **itemTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **commissionableAmount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **unitId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Unit'`

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code. We will look up the product

- **itemDescription**: `Text`

- **sortOrder**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **transactionDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **transactionDescription**: `Text`

- **amount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **gatewayName**: `Text`

- **gatewayTransactionId**: `Text`

- **historicalData**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass true if this is not actual transaction. Should be False by default
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | true | true |
  | false | false |
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "linka",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createInvoice",

      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **overrideLists**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will override lists of contact details in update mode instead of merging them - lists, tags, emails, phones, links, addresses, photos.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

- **ignoreInvalidValues**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will save the record even if there are some validation errors.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  This is string external reference that can be passed during creation and then if sent again it will update the record.

- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **createUser**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then User will be created. Personal email will be used as User Name.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **sendWelcomeEmail**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then Welcome Email will be sent to the newly created user.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **userPassword**: `Text`
  If password is not passed then it will be automatically generated.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **drivingLicense**: `Text`

- **drivingLicenseState**: `Text`

- **isActiveMilitaryDuty**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **isUSCitizen**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **preferredToD**: `StaticDropdown`
  Preferred Time of Day to contact with Client
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Morning | 'Morning' |
  | Afternoon | 'Afternoon' |
  | Evening | 'Evening' |
  | Anytime | 'Anytime' |

- **personAffiliateCode**: `Text`
  Affiliate Code is used for the current person detection as a source of new leads. Alphanumeric characters, underscore and hyphen are allowed.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative personal email.

- **email3**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **workEmail2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work email.

- **workEmail3**: `Text`
  The contact's other work email.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's primary phone number.

- **mobilePhoneExt**: `Text`
  The contact's primary phone number extension.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **homePhoneExt**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number extension.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work phone number.

- **workPhone1Ext**: `Text`
  The contact's work phone number extension.

- **workPhone2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number.

- **workPhone2Ext**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number extension.

- **home_street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **home_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **home_city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **home_stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **home_stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **home_zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **home_countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **home_countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **work_street**: `Text`
  The contact's work address.

- **work_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **work_city**: `Text`
  The contact's work city.

- **work_stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's work state.

- **work_stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's work state code.

- **work_zip**: `Text`
  The contact's work zip code.

- **work_countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's work country.

- **work_countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's work country code.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **facebookUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Facebook profile id.

- **instagramUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Instagram profile id.

- **twitterUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Twitter profile id.

- **googlePlusUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Google reviews.

- **angelListUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's AngelList profile id.

- **zoomUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Zoom id.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **customField1**: `Text`
  Additional custom data for the contact record.

- **customField2**: `Text`

- **customField3**: `Text`

- **customField4**: `Text`

- **customField5**: `Text`

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **organizationType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | LLP | 'LLP' |
  | LLC | 'LLC' |

- **applicantId**: `Text`

- **applicationId**: `Text`

- **userAgent**: `Text`

- **siteId**: `Text`

- **siteUrl**: `Text`

- **dateCreated**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **leadStageName**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **star**: `Text`
  String Value. Supports the following items: Yellow, Blue, Green, Purple, Red. Other values will be skipped.

- **rating**: `Text`
  This is the static array from 1 to 10

  Product Code from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |

- **sub1_systemType**: `Text`
  Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

- **sub1_code**: `Text`
  Code of subscription service from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

- **sub1_name**: `Text`

- **sub1_level**: `Text`
  Code of subscription service level from the Sperse CRM.

- **sub1_startDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS.

- **sub1_endDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS.

### Add or Update Subscription

Creates a new subscription.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **productId**: `Number`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  ContactXref have to be specified and correct to look up the correct contact

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code (Unique product identifier). ProductCode have to be specified and correct to look up the correct product
  **Required**: Yes

- **paymentPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **hasRecurringBilling**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "linka",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateSubscription",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "productId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "paymentPeriodType": "'Monthly'",
      "hasRecurringBilling": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Create Product

Creates a new product in the CRM

#### Parameters
- **productType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | General | 'General' |
  | Event | 'Event' |
  | Subscription | 'Subscription' |
  | Digital | 'Digital' |
  Default value: `'General'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **code**: `Text`
  Sku is the product code
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **descriptionHTML**: `Text`
  Javascript and media tags are not allowed

- **logoURL**: `Text`

- **groupName**: `Text`

- **price**: `Number`
  Required for General , Digital and Event Product Type
  Default value: `0`

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`

- **unit**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Day'`

- **frequency**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  | OneTime | 'OneTime' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`

- **fee**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **cycles**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **signupFee**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **customPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Days | 'Days' |
  | Weeks | 'Weeks' |
  | Months | 'Months' |
  | Years | 'Years' |
  Default value: `'Days'`

- **customPeriodCount**: `Number`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Default value: `0`

- **trialDayCount**: `Number`
  Required for OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **gracePeriodDayCount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "linka",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createProduct",
    "input": {
      "productType": "'General'",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "code": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "descriptionHTML": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "logoURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "groupName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "price": 0,
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "unit": "'Day'",
      "frequency": "'Monthly'",
      "fee": 0,
      "cycles": 0,
      "signupFee": 0,
      "customPeriodType": "'Days'",
      "customPeriodCount": 0,
      "trialDayCount": 0,
      "gracePeriodDayCount": 0
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# LocalAI

The free, Self-hosted, community-driven and local-first. Drop-in replacement for OpenAI running on consumer-grade hardware. No GPU required.

## Actions

### Ask LocalAI

The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Parameters
- **model**: `Dropdown`
  The model which will generate the completion. Some models are suitable for natural language tasks, others specialize in code.
  Default value: `'gpt-3.5-turbo'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

- **topP**: `Number`
  An alternative to sampling with temperature, called nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered.

- **frequencyPenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far, decreasing the model's likelihood to repeat the same line verbatim.

- **presencePenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far, increasing the mode's likelihood to talk about new topics.

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response
  Default value: `[`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "localai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask_localai",
    "input": {
      "model": "'gpt-3.5-turbo'",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "temperature": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "maxTokens": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "topP": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "frequencyPenalty": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "presencePenalty": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "roles": "["
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# MessageBird

Next generation CRM for Marketing, Services and Payments

## Actions

### Send SMS

Enter the sender details. You can either enter the sender's phone number with country code or name or text that is alphanumeric.

#### Parameters
- **originator**: `Text`
  Enter the sender details. You can either enter the sender's phone number with country code or name or text that is alphanumeric.
  **Required**: Yes

- **body**: `Text`
  The body of the SMS message.
  **Required**: Yes

- **recipients**: `Array`
  Enter the recipient number to whom you want to send the message.
  **Required**: Yes

- **datacoding**: `StaticDropdown`
  Using unicode will limit the maximum number of characters to 70 instead of 160.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Auto | 'auto' |
  | Plain | 'plain' |
  | Unicode | 'unicode' |

- **gateway**: `Number`
  The SMS route that is used to send the message.

- **validity**: `Number`
  The amount of seconds that the message is valid. If a message is not delivered within this time, the message will be discarded.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "messagebird",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send-sms",
    "input": {
      "originator": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "body": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recipients": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "datacoding": "'auto'",
      "gateway": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "validity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

  Refers to your username or organization name with which you signed up with.
  Default value: `'mindee'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **api_name**: `StaticDropdown`
  Refers to the name of the API your are using.
  Default value: `'full'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **file**: `Text`

  **Required**: Yes

```json
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},

    }
```

# Mixpanel

Simple and powerful product analytics that helps everyone make better decisions

## Actions

### Track Event

A name for this Event. For example, 'Brand Mentioned in Tweet' or 'Payment Made'.

#### Parameters
- **event**: `Text`
  A name for this Event. For example, 'Brand Mentioned in Tweet' or 'Payment Made'.
  **Required**: Yes

- **distinct_id**: `Text`
  A way to uniquely identify your users (or more generally, profiles). If you are sending Profiles to Mixpanel in addition to events, this property value should be identical to the Distinct ID property attached to the Profile so that you can connect events to people records.

- **event_properties**: `Object`
  Event Properties are bits of extra information that you send along with your Events describing the details of that action. They are usually specific to the Event they’re describing and don’t apply universally to other Events. Leveraging Event Properties allows you to conduct deeper analysis to better understand user behavior for a specific action. For example, a 'Song Added to Playlist' event could have 'Artist' and 'Playlist' as the properties. Properties are sent as key-value pairs where the key is the property name and the value is the property value.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "mixpanel",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "track_event",
    "input": {
      "event": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "distinct_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_properties": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Moxie

CRM build for the freelancers.

## Actions

### Create a Project

Creates a new project in moxie CRM.

#### Parameters
- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **clientName**: `Dropdown`
  **Required**: Yes

- **startDate**: `DateTime`
  Please enter date in YYYY-MM-DD format.

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  Please enter date in YYYY-MM-DD format.

- **portalAccess**: `StaticDropdown`
  One of: None, Overview, Full access, or Read only.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Not Visible | 'None' |
  | Overview only | 'Overview' |
  | Read only project collaboration | 'Read |
  | Full project collaboration | 'Full |
  Default value: `'Read`
  **Required**: Yes

- **showTimeWorkedInPortal**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `True`

- **feeType**: `StaticDropdown`
  One of: Hourly, Fixed Price, Retainer, Per Item.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Hourly | 'Hourly' |
  | Fixed Price | 'Fixed |
  | Retainer | 'Retainer' |
  | Per Item | 'Per |
  **Required**: Yes

- **amount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **estimateMax**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **estimateMin**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **taxable**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "moxie",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "moxie_create_project",
    "input": {
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "clientName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "startDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "dueDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "portalAccess": "'None'",
      "showTimeWorkedInPortal": true,
      "feeType": "'Hourly'",
      "amount": 0,
      "estimateMax": 0,
      "estimateMin": 0,
      "taxable": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Create a Task

Create a task in project.

#### Parameters
- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **clientName**: `Dropdown`
  Exact match of a client name in your CRM
  **Required**: Yes

- **projectName**: `Dropdown`
  Exact match of a project that is owned by the client.
  **Required**: Yes

- **status**: `Dropdown`
  Default value: `'Not`
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **startDate**: `DateTime`
  ISO 8601 format date i.e. 2023-07-20

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  ISO 8601 format date i.e. 2023-07-20

- **priority**: `Number`
  Numeric priority for sorting in kanban.

- **tasks**: `Array`

- **assignedTo**: `Array`
  email addresses of users in the workspace.

- **customValues**: `Object`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "moxie",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "moxie_create_task",
    "input": {
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "clientName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "projectName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "'Not",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "startDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "dueDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "priority": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tasks": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "assignedTo": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "customValues": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

```json
      "postal": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "country": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "website": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "color": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "taxId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadSource": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "archive": false,
      "payInstructions": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "hourlyAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "roundingIncrement": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "currency": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stripeClientId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
```

```json
    "type": "WEBHOOK",
    "settings": {
      "md": null

  }
}
```

- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

  **Required**: Yes

- **markdown**: `Boolean`
  Convert Notion JSON blocks to Markdown
  Default value: `False`

  **Required**: Yes

  Default value: `1`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example

```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "notion",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "getPageOrBlockChildren",
    "input": {
      "parentId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "markdown": false,
      "dynamic": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "depth": 1
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# ntfy

Notification management made easy

## Actions

### Send Notification

Let ntfy send messages at a later date, e.g. 'tomorrow, 10am', see https://docs.ntfy.sh/publish/#scheduled-delivery

#### Parameters
- **topic**: `Text`
  The topic/channel to send the notification to, e.g. test1
  **Required**: Yes

- **title**: `Text`
  The title of the notification

- **message**: `Text`
  The message to send
  **Required**: Yes

- **priority**: `Text`
  The priority of the notification (1-5). 1 is lowest priority.

- **tags**: `Array`
  The tags for the notification.

- **icon**: `Text`
  The absolute URL to your icon, e.g. https://example.com/communityIcon_xnt6chtnr2j21.png

- **actions**: `Text`
  Add Action buttons to notifications, see https://docs.ntfy.sh/publish/#action-buttons

- **click**: `Text`
  You can define which URL to open when a notification is clicked, see https://docs.ntfy.sh/publish/#click-action

- **delay**: `Text`
  Let ntfy send messages at a later date, e.g. 'tomorrow, 10am', see https://docs.ntfy.sh/publish/#scheduled-delivery

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ntfy",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send_notification",
    "input": {
      "topic": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "message": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "priority": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "icon": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "actions": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "click": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "delay": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Recipient

The recipient's full name

#### Parameters
- **name**: `Text`
  The recipient's full name
  **Required**: Yes

- **phone**: `Text`
  A unique, valid phone number as per the organization's country if there's no leading + sign. If a phone number has a leading + sign, it will disregard the organization's country setting.
  **Required**: Yes

- **notes**: `Text`

- **skipSMSNotifications**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

- **skipPhoneNumberValidation**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

- **useLongCodeForText**: `Boolean`
  Checking this option will default the Onfleet system to use a toll-free long code number for SMS communication.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "onfleet",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_recipient",
    "input": {
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "skipSMSNotifications": false,
      "skipPhoneNumberValidation": false,
      "useLongCodeForText": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Task

The recipient's full name

#### Parameters
- **merchant**: `Text`
  ID of the organization that will be displayed on the task

- **executor**: `Text`
  ID of the organization that will be executing the task

- **recipient**: `DynamicProperties`
  The task destination
  **Required**: Yes

- **id**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  The recipient's full name
  **Required**: Yes

- **phone**: `Text`
  A unique, valid phone number as per the organization's country if there's no leading + sign. If a phone number has a leading + sign, it will disregard the organization's country setting.
  **Required**: Yes

- **notes**: `Text`

- **skipSMSNotifications**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

- **useRecipientID**: `Boolean`
  Check this box if you want to use an ID for the recipient
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **completeAfter**: `DateTime`
  The earliest time the task should be completed

- **completeBefore**: `DateTime`
  The latest time the task should be completed

- **pickupTask**: `Boolean`
  Whether the task is pickup

- **quantity**: `Number`
  The number of units to be dropped off

- **recipientName**: `Text`
  Override the recipient name for this task only

- **recipientNotes**: `Text`
  Override the recipient notes for this task only

- **recipientSkipSMSNotifications**: `Boolean`
  Override the recipient skip SMS option for this task only

- **serviceTime**: `Number`
  The number of minutes to be spent by the worker on arrival at this task's destination

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "onfleet",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_task",
    "input": {
      "merchant": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "executor": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recipient": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "phone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "skipSMSNotifications": false,
      "useRecipientID": false,
      "completeAfter": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "completeBefore": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "pickupTask": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "quantity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recipientName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recipientNotes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recipientSkipSMSNotifications": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "serviceTime": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# OpenRouter

Use any AI model to generate code, text, or images via OpenRouter.ai.

## Actions

### Ask LLM

The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Parameters
- **model**: `Dropdown`
  The model which will generate the completion. Some models are suitable for natural language tasks, others specialize in code.
  Default value: `'pygmalionai/mythalion-13b'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  The prompt to send to the model.
  **Required**: Yes

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

- **topP**: `Number`
  An alternative to sampling with temperature, called nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "openrouter",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask-lmm",
    "input": {
      "model": "'pygmalionai/mythalion-13b'",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "temperature": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "maxTokens": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "topP": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

```json
  "valid": true,

    "pieceName": "openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "transcribe",

      "audio": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "language": "'en'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},

    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
```

### Extract Structured Data from Text

Returns structured data from provided unstructured text.

#### Parameters
- **model**: `Dropdown`
  Default value: `'gpt-3.5-turbo'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **text**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **params**: `Array`
  **Required**: Yes

- **propName**: `Text`
  Provide the name of the value you want to extract from the unstructured text. The name should be unique and short.
  **Required**: Yes

- **propDescription**: `Text`
  Brief description of the data, this hints for the AI on what to look for

- **propDataType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Type of parameter.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Text | 'string' |
  | Number | 'number' |
  | Boolean | 'boolean' |
  Default value: `'string'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **propIsRequired**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "extract-structured-data",
    "input": {
      "model": "'gpt-3.5-turbo'",
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "params": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "propName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "propDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "propDataType": "'string'",
      "propIsRequired": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### Vision Prompt

The image URL or file you want GPT's vision to read.

#### Parameters
- **image**: `File`
  The image URL or file you want GPT's vision to read.
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  What do you want ChatGPT to tell you about the image?
  **Required**: Yes

- **detail**: `Dropdown`
  Control how the model processes the image and generates textual understanding.
  Default value: `'auto'`

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.
  Default value: `0.9`

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion, don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. The exact limit varies by model. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text
  Default value: `2048`

- **topP**: `Number`
  An alternative to sampling with temperature, called nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered.
  Default value: `1`

- **frequencyPenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far, decreasing the model's likelihood to repeat the same line verbatim.
  Default value: `0`

- **presencePenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far, increasing the mode's likelihood to talk about new topics.
  Default value: `0.6`

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response
  Default value: `[`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "vision_prompt",
    "input": {
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "detail": "'auto'",
      "temperature": 0.9,
      "maxTokens": 2048,
      "topP": 1,
      "frequencyPenalty": 0,
      "presencePenalty": 0.6,
      "roles": "["
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Ask ChatGPT

The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion depending on the model. Don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text

#### Parameters
- **model**: `Dropdown`
  The model which will generate the completion. Some models are suitable for natural language tasks, others specialize in code.
  Default value: `'gpt-3.5-turbo'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **temperature**: `Number`
  Controls randomness: Lowering results in less random completions. As the temperature approaches zero, the model will become deterministic and repetitive.
  Default value: `0.9`

- **maxTokens**: `Number`
  The maximum number of tokens to generate. Requests can use up to 2,048 or 4,096 tokens shared between prompt and completion depending on the model. Don't set the value to maximum and leave some tokens for the input. (One token is roughly 4 characters for normal English text
  Default value: `2048`
  **Required**: Yes

- **topP**: `Number`
  An alternative to sampling with temperature, called nucleus sampling, where the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass are considered.
  Default value: `1`

- **frequencyPenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far, decreasing the model's likelihood to repeat the same line verbatim.
  Default value: `0`

- **presencePenalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far, increasing the mode's likelihood to talk about new topics.
  Default value: `0.6`

- **memoryKey**: `Text`
  A memory key that will keep the chat history shared across runs and flows. Keep it empty to leave ChatGPT without memory of previous messages.

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response
  Default value: `[`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask_chatgpt",
    "input": {
      "model": "'gpt-3.5-turbo'",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "temperature": 0.9,
      "maxTokens": 2048,
      "topP": 1,
      "frequencyPenalty": 0,
      "presencePenalty": 0.6,
      "memoryKey": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "roles": "["
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Text-to-Speech

Generate an audio recording from text

#### Parameters
- **text**: `Text`
  The text you want to hear.
  **Required**: Yes

- **model**: `Dropdown`
  The model which will generate the audio.
  Default value: `'tts-1'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **speed**: `Number`
  The speed of the audio. Minimum is 0.25 and maximum is 4.00.
  Default value: `1.0`

- **voice**: `Dropdown`
  The voice to generate the audio in.
  Default value: `'alloy'`

- **format**: `Dropdown`
  The format you want the audio file in.
  Default value: `'mp3'`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "openai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "text_to_speech",
    "input": {
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "model": "'tts-1'",
      "speed": 1.0,
      "voice": "'alloy'",
      "format": "'mp3'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
```

# Perplexity AI

AI powered search engine

## Actions

### Ask AI

Please refer [guide](https://docs.perplexity.ai/guides/model-cards) for each model token limit.

#### Parameters
- **model**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | llama-3.1-sonar-small-128k-online | 'llama-3.1-sonar-small-128k-online' |
  | llama-3.1-sonar-large-128k-online | 'llama-3.1-sonar-large-128k-online' |
  | llama-3.1-sonar-huge-128k-online | 'llama-3.1-sonar-huge-128k-online' |
  | llama-3.1-sonar-small-128k-chat | 'llama-3.1-sonar-small-128k-chat' |
  | llama-3.1-sonar-large-128k-chat | 'llama-3.1-sonar-large-128k-chat' |
  | llama-3.1-8b-instruct | 'llama-3.1-8b-instruct' |
  | llama-3.1-70b-instruct | 'llama-3.1-70b-instruct' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **prompt**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **temperature**: `Number`
  The amount of randomness in the response.Higher values are more random, and lower values are more deterministic.
  Default value: `0.2`

- **max_tokens**: `Number`
  Please refer [guide](https://docs.perplexity.ai/guides/model-cards) for each model token limit.

- **top_p**: `Number`
  The nucleus sampling threshold, valued between 0 and 1 inclusive. For each subsequent token, the model considers the results of the tokens with top_p probability mass.
  Default value: `0.9`

- **presence_penalty**: `Number`
  Number between -2.0 and 2.0. Positive values penalize new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far, increasing the mode's likelihood to talk about new topics.
  Default value: `0`

- **frequency_penalty**: `Number`
  A multiplicative penalty greater than 0. Values greater than 1.0 penalize new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far, decreasing the model's likelihood to repeat the same line verbatim.
  Default value: `1.0`

- **roles**: `JSON`
  Array of roles to specify more accurate response.After the (optional) system message, user and assistant roles should alternate with user then assistant, ending in user.
  Default value: `[`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "perplexity-ai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "ask-ai",
    "input": {
      "model": "'llama-3.1-sonar-small-128k-online'",
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "temperature": 0.2,
      "max_tokens": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "top_p": 0.9,
      "presence_penalty": 0,
      "frequency_penalty": 1.0,
      "roles": "["
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

# Postgres

The world's most advanced open-source relational database

## Actions

### Run Query

Run Query

#### Parameters
- **markdown**: `MarkDown`

- **query**: `Text`
  Please use $1, $2, etc. for parameterized queries to avoid SQL injection.
  **Required**: Yes

- **args**: `Array`
  Arguments to be used in the query

- **query_timeout**: `Number`
  An integer indicating the maximum number of milliseconds to wait for a query to complete before timing out.
  Default value: `30000`

- **connection_timeout_ms**: `Number`
  An integer indicating the maximum number of milliseconds to wait for a connection to be established before timing out.
  Default value: `30000`

- **application_name**: `Text`
  A string indicating the name of the client application connecting to the server.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "postgres",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "run-query",
    "input": {
      "markdown": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "query": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "args": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "query_timeout": 30000,
      "connection_timeout_ms": 30000,
      "application_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Event

User's Distinct Id

#### Parameters
- **event**: `Text`
  The event name
  **Required**: Yes

- **event_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Alias | 'alias' |
  | Capture | 'capture' |
  | Identify | 'screen' |
  | Page | 'page' |
  | Screen | 'screen' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **distinct_id**: `Text`
  User's Distinct Id
  **Required**: Yes

- **properties**: `Object`
  The event properties

- **context**: `Object`
  The event context,

- **message_id**: `Text`
  The message id,

- **category**: `Text`
  The event category.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "posthog",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_event",
    "input": {
      "event": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "event_type": "'alias'",
      "distinct_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "properties": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "context": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "message_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "category": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```
