# Pushover

Simple push notification service

## Actions

### Send Notification

Send a notification to Pushover

#### Parameters
- **title**: `Text`
  The title of the notification

- **message**: `Text`
  The message to send
  **Required**: Yes

- **html**: `Boolean`
  To enable HTML parsing

- **priority**: `Number`
  The priority of the notification (-2 to 2). -2 is lowest priority. If set to 2, you should also specify Retry and Expire.

- **retry**: `Number`
  Works only if priority is set to 2. Specifies how often (in seconds) the Pushover servers will send the same notification to the user.

- **expire**: `Number`
  Works only if priority is set to 2. Specifies how many seconds your notification will continue to be retried for (every retry seconds).

- **url**: `Text`
  A supplementary URL to show with your message.

- **url_title**: `Text`
  A title for the URL specified as the url input parameter, otherwise just the URL is shown.

- **timestamp**: `Text`
  a Unix timestamp of a time to display instead of when our API received it.

- **device**: `Text`
  The name of one of your devices to send just to that device instead of all devices.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "pushover",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send_notification",
    "input": {
      "title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "message": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "html": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "priority": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "retry": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "expire": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "url": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "url_title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "timestamp": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "device": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

```json
      "queue": null,
```

### Set Schedule

Update the schedule for a specific Campaign

#### Parameters
- **campaignId**: `Dropdown`
  Choose a campaign from the list or enter the campaign ID manually.
  **Required**: Yes

- **scheduleName**: `Text`
  Enter the schedule name here (e.g., New schedule).
  **Required**: Yes

- **startDate**: `DateTime`
  Enter the start date (e.g., 2023-08-01T00:00:00.000Z).
  **Required**: Yes

- **endDate**: `DateTime`
  Enter the end date (e.g., 2024-08-25T00:00:00.000Z).
  **Required**: Yes

- **startTime**: `Text`
  Enter the start time (e.g., 09:00).
  **Required**: Yes

- **endTime**: `Text`
  Enter the end time (e.g., 12:00).
  **Required**: Yes

- **timezone**: `Text`
  Enter the timezone (e.g., America/Detroit).
  **Required**: Yes

- **sunday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Sunday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **monday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Monday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **tuesday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Tuesday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **wednesday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Wednesday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **thursday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Thursday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **friday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Friday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **saturday**: `Boolean`
  Choose "Yes" if you want to set a schedule for Saturday.
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "reachinbox",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "setSchedule",
    "input": {
      "campaignId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "scheduleName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "startDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "endDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "startTime": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "endTime": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "timezone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sunday": false,
      "monday": false,
      "tuesday": false,
      "wednesday": false,
      "thursday": false,
      "friday": false,
      "saturday": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

  **Required**: Yes

  **Required**: Yes

  Notification Email.

- **success_email**: `Text`

- **success_message**: `Text`

- **error_message**: `Text`

### Find Company Paths

If you're a Village Partner, use this field that identifies your user

#### Parameters
- **user_identifier**: `Text`
  If you're a Village Partner, use this field that identifies your user

- **company_domain_url**: `Text`
  The Company Domain URL of the company you're trying to find paths to. E.g. https://openai.com/

- **company_linkedin_url**: `Text`
  The Company Linkedin URL of the company you're trying to find paths to. E.g. https://www.linkedin.com/company/openai/

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "village",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "fetchCompaniesPaths",
    "input": {
      "user_identifier": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "company_domain_url": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "company_linkedin_url": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Vtiger

CRM software for sales, marketing, and support teams

## Actions

### Query Records

Query records by SQL statement.

#### Parameters
- **query**: `Text`
  Enter the query statement, e.g. SELECT count(*) FROM Contacts;
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "vtiger",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "query_records",
    "input": {
      "query": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Custom API Call

Enter the desired request headers. Skip the authorization headers

#### Parameters
- **headers**: `JSON`
  Enter the desired request headers. Skip the authorization headers
  Default value: `{`
  **Required**: Yes

- **data**: `JSON`
  Enter the data to pass. if its POST, it will be sent as body data, and if GET, as query string
  Default value: `{`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "vtiger",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "make_api_call",
    "input": {
      "headers": "{",
      "data": "{"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Webhook

Receive HTTP requests and trigger flows using unique URLs.

## Actions

### Return Response

return a response

#### Parameters
- **responseType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | JSON | ResponseType.JSON |
  | Raw | ResponseType.RAW |
  | Redirect | ResponseType.REDIRECT |
  Default value: `'json'`

- **fields**: `DynamicProperties`
  Default value: `200`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "webhook",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "return_response",
    "input": {
      "responseType": "ResponseType.JSON",
      "fields": 200
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

## Triggers

### Catch Webhook

Receive incoming HTTP/webhooks using any HTTP method such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, etc.

#### Parameters
- **liveMarkdown**: `MarkDown`

- **syncMarkdown**: `MarkDown`

- **testMarkdown**: `MarkDown`

- **authFields**: `DynamicProperties`

- **username**: `Text`
  The username to use for authentication.
  **Required**: Yes

- **password**: `Text`
  The password to use for authentication.
  **Required**: Yes

- **headerName**: `Text`
  The name of the header to use for authentication.
  **Required**: Yes

- **headerValue**: `Text`
  The value to check against the header.
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "trigger": {
    "valid": true,
    "type": "WEBHOOK",
    "settings": {
      "liveMarkdown": null,
      "syncMarkdown": null,
      "testMarkdown": null,
      "authFields": null,
      "username": null,
      "password": null,
      "headerName": null,
      "headerValue": null
    }
  }
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

# Webling
## Actions

### Get Events by ID

Comma seperated list of event IDs (e.g. '536,525,506,535'). When at least one ID doesn't exist the whole query return a 404 error.

#### Parameters
- **eventIds**: `Text`
  Comma seperated list of event IDs (e.g. '536,525,506,535'). When at least one ID doesn't exist the whole query return a 404 error.
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "webling",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "EventsById",
    "input": {
      "eventIds": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### (Période) et jusqu'au

Permet de filtrer les dossiers de certification qui sont exclus de l'accrochage

#### Parameters
- **query**: `Text`
  Nom, prénom, N° de dossier, N° de certification etc..

- **periodForm**: `DynamicProperties`
  **Required**: Yes

- **cdcExcluded**: `StaticDropdown`
  Permet de filtrer les dossiers de certification qui sont exclus de l'accrochage

- **cdcCompliant**: `StaticDropdown`
  Permet de filtrer les dossiers de certification selon le fait qu'ils contiennent les données de l'apprenant obligatoires pour l'accrochage en cas d'obtention de la certification

- **cdcToExport**: `StaticDropdown`
  Permet de filtrer les dossiers de certification qui devront être inclus dans les prochains exports pour l'accrochage (par défaut oui, sauf si déjà accroché avec succès

- **limit**: `Number`
  Nombre de dossiers de certification maximum qui seront retournés par requête
  Default value: `100`

- **page**: `Number`
  Par défaut : 1
  Default value: `1`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "wedof",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "searchCertificationFolder",
    "input": {
      "query": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "periodForm": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cdcExcluded": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cdcCompliant": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cdcToExport": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "limit": 100,
      "page": 1
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Tiers temps

Met à jour certaines informations modifiables d'un dossier de certification

#### Parameters
- **externalId**: `Text`
  Sélectionner la propriété {externalId} du dossier de certification
  **Required**: Yes

- **enrollmentDate**: `DateTime`
  Date au format YYYY-MM-DD

- **examinationDate**: `DateTime`
  Date au format YYYY-MM-DD

- **examinationEndDate**: `DateTime`
  Date au format YYYY-MM-DD

- **examinationPlace**: `Text`
  Lieu de l'examen de certification (ou lien https

- **tiersTemps**: `StaticDropdown`
  Indique si le candidat a besoin d'un tiers temps
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Non | false |
  | Oui | true |
  **Required**: Yes

- **comment**: `Text`
  Commentaire (non-visible par l'apprenant

- **verbatim**: `Text`
  Verbatim

- **amountHt**: `Number`
  Tarif en €

- **tags**: `Array`
  Liste de tags associée au dossier de certification, si vous souhaitez garder vos précédents tags, il faut les réécrire dans le champ

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "wedof",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "updateCertificationFolder",
    "input": {
      "externalId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "enrollmentDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "examinationDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "examinationEndDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "examinationPlace": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tiersTemps": "false",
      "comment": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "verbatim": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "amountHt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

```json
    "pieceName": "wedof",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "refuseCertificationFolder",
    "input": {
      "externalId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "comment": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",

    }
```

### Nombre d'enquêtes

Récupérer l'ensemble des enquêtes de l'organisme de l'utilisateur connecté

#### Parameters
- **certifInfo**: `Text`
  Permet de n'obtenir que les enquêtes liées à la certification considérée

- **limit**: `Text`
  Nombre d'éléments retourné par requête - par défaut 100

- **order**: `StaticDropdown`
  Tri les résultats par ordre ascendant ou descendant

- **page**: `Number`
  Par défaut : 1
  Default value: `1`

- **state**: `StaticDropdown`
  Permet de n'obtenir que les enquêtes en fonction de l'état considéré

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "wedof",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "listCertificationFolderSurveys",
    "input": {
      "certifInfo": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "limit": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "order": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "page": 1,
      "state": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

- **periodForm**: `DynamicProperties`
  **Required**: Yes

- **proposalCode**: `Text`
  Code de la proposition commercial Wedof associé

- **limit**: `Number`
  Nombre de dossiers de formation maximum qui seront retournés par requête

```json
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},

      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
```

### Taux d'avancement

Met à jour certaines informations modifiables d'un dossier de formation

#### Parameters
- **externalId**: `Text`
  Sélectionner la propriété {externalId} du dossier de formation
  **Required**: Yes

- **price**: `Number`
  Nouveau tarif en €

- **sessionStartDate**: `DateTime`
  Date au format YYYY-MM-DD

- **sessionEndDate**: `DateTime`
  Date au format YYYY-MM-DD

- **notes**: `Text`
  Notes privées (non-visible par l'apprenant

- **completionRate**: `Number`
  Taux d'avancement en % compris entre 0% et 100%. Uniquement sous format d'un entier. Uniquement possible à l'état En formation et Sortie de formation

- **indicativeDuration**: `Number`
  En heures, durée moyenne de la formation

- **weeklyDuration**: `Number`
  En heures, ne peut pas être supérieur à 99

- **tags**: `Array`
  Liste de tags associée au dossier de formation, si vous souhaitez garder vos précédents tags, il faut les réécrire dans le champ

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "wedof",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "updateRegistrationFolder",
    "input": {
      "externalId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "price": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sessionStartDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sessionEndDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "completionRate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "indicativeDuration": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "weeklyDuration": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

## Triggers

### Nouveau dossier de certification

Se déclenche lorsqu'un nouveau dossier de certification est créé

---


### Événement sur le dossier de certification

Se déclenche lorsque l'événement choisi se produit sur un dossier de certification

---


### Dossier de certification réussi

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation passe à l'état réussi

---


### Dossier de certification mis à jour

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de certification est mis à jour

---


### Dossier de certification à repasser

Se déclanche lorsqu'un dossier de certification est prét à repasser

---


### Dossier de certification prêt à passer

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de certification est prét à passer

---


### Dossier de certification enregistré

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de certification est enregistré

---


### Dossier de certification à contrôler

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de certification passe à controler

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle au moins un an" répondue

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de au moins un an de cursus est répondue

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle de 6 mois" disponible

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de 6 mois de cursus est disponible

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle en début de cursus" disponible

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de début de cursus est disponible

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle en début de cursus" répondue

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de début de cursus est répondue

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle au moins un an" disponible

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de au moins un an de cursus est disponible

---


### Enquête "Situation professionnelle de 6 mois" répondue

Se déclenche lorsqu'un une enquête de 6 mois de cursus est répondue

---


### Dossier de formation à facturer

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation est prêt à être facturé (service fait validé

---


### Dossier de formation mis à jour

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation est mis à jour

---


### Dossier de formation entre en formation

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation passe à l'état en formation

---


### Nouveau dossier de formation

Se déclenche lorsqu'un nouveau dossier de formation est créé (non traité

---


### Dossier de formation payé (acompte ou payé totalement

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation est payé

---


### Dossier de formation accepté

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation passe à l'état accepté

---


### Dossier de formation sort de formation

Se déclenche lorsqu'un dossier de formation passe à l'état sorti de formation

---


### Événement sur le dossier de formation

Se déclenche lorsque l'événement choisi se produit sur un dossier de formation

# SendGrid

Email delivery service for sending transactional and marketing emails

## Actions

### Send Email

Send a text or HTML email

#### Parameters
- **to**: `Array`
  Emails of the recipients
  **Required**: Yes

- **from**: `Text`
  Sender email, must be on your SendGrid
  **Required**: Yes

- **from_name**: `Text`
  Sender name

- **reply_to**: `Text`
  Email to receive replies on (defaults to sender

- **subject**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **content**: `Text`
  HTML is only allowed if you selected HTML as type
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sendgrid",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send_email",
    "input": {
      "to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "from": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "from_name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "reply_to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "subject": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "content": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Brevo

Formerly Sendinblue, is a SaaS solution for relationship marketing

## Actions

### Create or Update Contact

Email address of the user. Mandatory if "SMS" field is not passed in "attributes" parameter. Mobile Number in SMS field should be passed with proper country code. For example: {"SMS":"+91xxxxxxxxxx"} or {"SMS":"0091xxxxxxxxxx"}

#### Parameters
- **email**: `Text`
  Email address of the user. Mandatory if "SMS" field is not passed in "attributes" parameter. Mobile Number in SMS field should be passed with proper country code. For example: {"SMS":"+91xxxxxxxxxx"} or {"SMS":"0091xxxxxxxxxx"}
  **Required**: Yes

- **ext_id**: `Text`
  Pass your own Id to create a contact.

- **attributes**: `Object`
  Pass the set of attributes and their values. The attribute's parameter should be passed in capital letter while creating a contact. These attributes must be present in your SendinBlue account. For eg: {"FNAME":"Elly", "LNAME":"Roger"}
  Default value: `{`

- **email_blacklisted**: `Boolean`
  Set this field to blacklist the contact for emails (emailBlacklisted = true
  Default value: `False`

- **sms_blacklisted**: `Boolean`
  Set this field to blacklist the contact for SMS (smsBlacklisted = true
  Default value: `False`

- **list_ids**: `Array`
  Ids of the lists to add the contact to.
  Default value: `[]`

- **smtp_blacklist_sender**: `Boolean`
  transactional email forbidden sender for contact. Use only for email Contact ( only available if updateEnabled = true
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "brevo",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_or_update_contact",
    "input": {
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ext_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "attributes": "{",
      "email_blacklisted": false,
      "sms_blacklisted": false,
      "list_ids": "[]",
      "smtp_blacklist_sender": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Sendy

Self-hosted email marketing software

## Actions

### Unsubscribe Multiple Lists

The user's email

#### Parameters
- **lists**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  Select the lists to subscribe to
  **Required**: Yes

- **email**: `Text`
  The user's email
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sendy",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "unsubscribe_multiple",
    "input": {
      "lists": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Subscribe Multiple Lists

The user's email

#### Parameters
- **lists**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  Select the lists to subscribe to
  **Required**: Yes

- **email**: `Text`
  The user's email
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  The user's name

- **country**: `Text`
  The user's 2 letter country code

- **ipaddress**: `Text`
  The user's IP address

- **referrer**: `Text`
  The URL where the user signed up from

- **gdpr**: `Boolean`
  If you're signing up EU users in a GDPR compliant manner, set to true
  Default value: `True`

- **silent**: `Boolean`
  set to true if your list is 'Double opt-in' but you want to bypass that and signup the user to the list as 'Single Opt-in instead
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sendy",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "subscribe_multiple_lists",
    "input": {
      "lists": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "country": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ipaddress": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "referrer": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gdpr": true,
      "silent": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### Create Campaign

Create a new campaign

#### Parameters
- **fromEmail**: `Text`
  The email address the campaign will be sent from
  **Required**: Yes

- **fromName**: `Text`
  The name the campaign will be sent from
  **Required**: Yes

- **replyTo**: `Text`
  The email address that will be used for replies
  **Required**: Yes

- **title**: `Text`
  The title of the campaign
  **Required**: Yes

- **subject**: `Text`
  The subject of the campaign email
  **Required**: Yes

- **plainText**: `Text`
  The plain text version of the campaign email

- **html**: `Text`
  The HTML version of the campaign email
  **Required**: Yes

- **lists**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  Select lists to send the campaign to

- **excludeLists**: `MultiSelectDropdown`
  Select lists to exclude from the campaign send

- **segments**: `Text`
  Comma separated list of segment IDs to send the campaign to

- **excludeSegments**: `Text`
  Comma separated list of segment IDs to exclude from the campaign send

- **queryString**: `Text`
  The query string to append to the campaign URL

- **trackOpens**: `StaticDropdown`
  Enable open tracking
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Disable | '0' |
  | Enable | '1' |
  | Anonymous | '2' |
  Default value: `'1'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **trackClicks**: `StaticDropdown`
  Enable click tracking
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Disable | '0' |
  | Enable | '1' |
  | Anonymous | '2' |
  Default value: `'1'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **autoSend**: `Boolean`
  Automatically send the campaign after creation
  Default value: `False`

- **schedule**: `DateTime`
  Schedule the campaign to be sent at a specific date and time. Date/time format: 2023-06-09T12:00:00Z

- **timezone**: `StaticDropdown`
  The timezone to use for the schedule
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Africa/Abidjan | 'Africa/Abidjan' |

### Subscribe Updated

The user's email

#### Parameters
- **list**: `Dropdown`
  Select the list to subscribe to
  **Required**: Yes

- **email**: `Text`
  The user's email
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  The user's name

- **country**: `Text`
  The user's 2 letter country code

- **ipaddress**: `Text`
  The user's IP address

- **referrer**: `Text`
  The URL where the user signed up from

- **gdpr**: `Boolean`
  If you're signing up EU users in a GDPR compliant manner, set to true
  Default value: `True`

- **silent**: `Boolean`
  set to true if your list is 'Double opt-in' but you want to bypass that and signup the user to the list as 'Single Opt-in instead
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sendy",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "subscribe",
    "input": {
      "list": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "country": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ipaddress": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "referrer": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gdpr": true,
      "silent": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

  **Required**: Yes

- **fileContent**: `File`
  **Required**: Yes

```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Folder

Creates a folder at given path.

#### Parameters
- **folderPath**: `Text`
  The new folder path e.g. `./myfolder`. For FTP/FTPS, it will create nested folders if necessary.
  **Required**: Yes

- **recursive**: `Boolean`
  For SFTP only: Create parent directories if they do not exist
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ftp/sftp",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createFolder",
    "input": {
      "folderPath": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recursive": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Rename File or Folder

Renames a file or folder at given path.

- **oldPath**: `Text`
  The path of the file or folder to rename e.g. `./myfolder/test.mp3

- **newPath**: `Text`

  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ftp/sftp",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "renameFileOrFolder",
    "input": {
      "information": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "oldPath": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "newPath": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Delete Folder

Deletes an existing folder at given path.

#### Parameters
- **folderPath**: `Text`
  The path of the folder to delete e.g. `./myfolder
  **Required**: Yes

- **recursive**: `Boolean`
  Enable this option to delete the folder and all its contents, including subfolders and files.
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "ftp/sftp",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "deleteFolder",
    "input": {
      "folderPath": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "recursive": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

## Triggers

### New File

Trigger when a new file is created or modified.

#### Parameters
- **path**: `Text`
  The path to watch for new files
  Default value: `'./'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **ignoreHiddenFiles**: `Boolean`
  Ignore hidden files
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "trigger": {
    "valid": true,
    "type": "POLLING",
    "settings": {
      "path": "'./'",
      "ignoreHiddenFiles": false
    }
  }
}
```

Available in next steps:
- `{{trigger.body}}` - Request body
- `{{trigger.headers}}` - Request headers
- `{{trigger.query}}` - Query parameters

Cloud-based subscription management platform that enables businesses to launch and monetize subscription services.

```json
      "continueOnFailure": false
```

### Create Invoice

Create a standalone invoice.

#### Parameters
- **accountNumber**: `Text`
  The number of the customer account associated with the invoice.
  **Required**: Yes

- **autoPay**: `Boolean`
  Whether invoices are automatically picked up for processing in the corresponding payment run.

- **comments**: `Text`

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  Provide YYYY-MM-DD format.
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceDate**: `DateTime`
  Provide YYYY-MM-DD format.
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceItems**: `Array`

- **productRatePlanChargeId**: `Text`
  The ID of the product rate plan charge that the invoice item is created from.You can use `Find Product Rate Plan` action to search associate rate plan charge.
  **Required**: Yes

- **amount**: `Number`
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **purchaseOrderNumber**: `Text`

- **quantity**: `Text`

- **serviceStartDate**: `Text`
  Provide YYYY-MM-DD format.
  **Required**: Yes

- **serviceEndDate**: `Text`
  Provide YYYY-MM-DD format.

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Draft | 'Draft' |
  | Posted | 'Posted' |
  Default value: `'Draft'`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "zuora",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create-invoice",
    "input": {
      "accountNumber": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "autoPay": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "comments": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "dueDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "invoiceDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "invoiceItems": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productRatePlanChargeId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "amount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "purchaseOrderNumber": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "quantity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "serviceStartDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "serviceEndDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "'Draft'"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

- **productImage**: `File`
  The public URL or the base64 image to use

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Active | ShopifyProductStatuses.ACTIVE |
  | Draft | ShopifyProductStatuses.DRAFT |
  | Archived | ShopifyProductStatuses.ARCHIVED |
  Default value: `ShopifyProductStatuses.DRAFT`
  **Required**: Yes

- **vendor**: `Text`

- **tags**: `Text`
  A string of comma-separated tags for filtering and search

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "shopify",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "create_product",
    "input": {
      "title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bodyHtml": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productType": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productImage": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "ShopifyProductStatuses.ACTIVE",
      "vendor": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Update Profile

Changing a user's email address will send an email to both the old and new addresses, and also post a slackbot message to the user informing them of the change.

#### Parameters
- **firstName**: `Text`

- **lastName**: `Text`

- **email**: `Text`
  Changing a user's email address will send an email to both the old and new addresses, and also post a slackbot message to the user informing them of the change.

- **userId**: `Text`
  ID of user to change. This argument may only be specified by admins on paid teams.You can use **Find User by Email** action to retrieve ID.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "slack",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "slack-update-profile",
    "input": {
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "userId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# SMTP

Send emails using Simple Mail Transfer Protocol

## Actions

### Sender Name

Send an email using a custom SMTP server.

#### Parameters
- **from**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **senderName**: `Text`

- **to**: `Array`
  **Required**: Yes

- **cc**: `Array`

- **replyTo**: `Text`

- **bcc**: `Array`

- **subject**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **body_type**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | plain text | 'plain_text' |
  | html | 'html' |
  Default value: `'plain_text'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **body**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **customHeaders**: `Object`

- **attachments**: `Array`

- **file**: `File`
  File to attach to the email you want to send
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  In case you want to change the name of the attachment

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "smtp",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "send-email",
    "input": {
      "from": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "senderName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "to": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cc": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "replyTo": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bcc": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "subject": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "body_type": "'plain_text'",
      "body": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "customHeaders": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "attachments": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "file": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Snowflake

Data warehouse built for the cloud

## Actions

### Insert Row

Insert a row into a table.

---


### Run Query

Run Query

#### Parameters
- **sqlText**: `Text`
  Use :1, :2… or ? placeholders to use binding parameters.
  **Required**: Yes

- **binds**: `Array`
  Binding parameters for the SQL query (to prevent SQL injection attacks

- **timeout**: `Number`
  An integer indicating the maximum number of milliseconds to wait for a query to complete before timing out.
  Default value: `DEFAULT_QUERY_TIMEOUT`

- **application**: `Text`
  A string indicating the name of the client application connecting to the server.
  Default value: `DEFAULT_APPLICATION_NAME`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "snowflake",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "runQuery",
    "input": {
      "sqlText": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "binds": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "timeout": "DEFAULT_QUERY_TIMEOUT",
      "application": "DEFAULT_APPLICATION_NAME"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

  | Label | Value |

  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **fullName**: `Text`
  The contact's full name.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **industry**: `Text`
  The company's industry.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work/primary phone number.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's mobile phone number.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **addressLine2**: `Text`

- **city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sperse",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateContact",
    "input": {
      "importType": "'Lead'",
      "matchExisting": "true",
      "contactId": 0,
      "fullName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "namePrefix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "middleName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nickName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nameSuffix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gender": "'Male'",
      "dob": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bankCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ssn": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "companyName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "jobTitle": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "industry": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workEmail1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workPhone1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "homePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "mobilePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "webSiteUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedInUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "photoUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "street": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "addressLine2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "city": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "zip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "experience": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "profileSummary": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "followUpDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "assignedUser": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadDealAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadSource": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "channelId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "affiliateCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "refererURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "entryUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",

      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Invoice

Creates a new invoice in the CRM.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  External Contact Reference (ID) . Will be used for looking a client

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Draft | 'Draft' |
  | Final | 'Final' |
  | Paid | 'Paid' |
  | Sent | 'Sent' |
  Default value: `'Draft'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceNo**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **date**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  **Required**: Yes

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **grandTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **discountTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **shippingTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **taxTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **bCompany**: `Text`

- **bFirstName**: `Text`

- **bLastName**: `Text`

- **bPhone**: `Text`

- **bEmail**: `Text`

- **bCountryId**: `Text`

- **bStateId**: `Text`

- **bStateName**: `Text`

- **bCity**: `Text`

- **bZip**: `Text`

- **bAddress1**: `Text`

- **bAddress2**: `Text`

- **sCompany**: `Text`

- **sFirstName**: `Text`

- **sLastName**: `Text`

- **sPhone**: `Text`

- **sEmail**: `Text`

- **sCountryId**: `Text`

- **sStateId**: `Text`

- **sStateName**: `Text`

- **sCity**: `Text`

- **sZip**: `Text`

- **sAddress1**: `Text`

- **sAddress2**: `Text`

- **note**: `Text`

- **invoiceDescription**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quantity**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **rate**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **itemTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **commissionableAmount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **unitId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Unit'`

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code. We will look up the product

- **itemDescription**: `Text`

- **sortOrder**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **transactionDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **transactionDescription**: `Text`

- **amount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **gatewayName**: `Text`

- **gatewayTransactionId**: `Text`

- **historicalData**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass true if this is not actual transaction. Should be False by default
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | true | true |
  | false | false |
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sperse",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createInvoice",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "'Draft'",
      "invoiceNo": 0,
      "date": "getCurrentDateInISOFormat()",
      "dueDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "grandTotal": 0,
      "discountTotal": 0,
      "shippingTotal": 0,
      "taxTotal": 0,
      "bCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bFirstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bZip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sFirstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sZip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sAddress1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sAddress2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "note": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "invoiceDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "quantity": 0,
      "rate": 0,
      "itemTotal": 0,
      "commissionableAmount": 0,
      "unitId": "'Unit'",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "itemDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sortOrder": 0,
      "transactionDate": "getCurrentDateInISOFormat()",
      "transactionDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "amount": 0,
      "gatewayName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gatewayTransactionId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "historicalData": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Product

Creates a new product in the CRM

#### Parameters
- **productType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | General | 'General' |
  | Event | 'Event' |
  | Subscription | 'Subscription' |
  | Digital | 'Digital' |
  Default value: `'General'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **code**: `Text`
  Sku is the product code
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **descriptionHTML**: `Text`
  Javascript and media tags are not allowed

- **logoURL**: `Text`

- **groupName**: `Text`

- **price**: `Number`
  Required for General , Digital and Event Product Type
  Default value: `0`

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`

- **unit**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Day'`

- **frequency**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  | OneTime | 'OneTime' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`

- **fee**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **cycles**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **signupFee**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **customPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Days | 'Days' |
  | Weeks | 'Weeks' |
  | Months | 'Months' |
  | Years | 'Years' |
  Default value: `'Days'`

- **customPeriodCount**: `Number`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Default value: `0`

- **trialDayCount**: `Number`
  Required for OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **gracePeriodDayCount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sperse",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createProduct",
    "input": {
      "productType": "'General'",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "code": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "descriptionHTML": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "logoURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "groupName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "price": 0,
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "unit": "'Day'",
      "frequency": "'Monthly'",
      "fee": 0,
      "cycles": 0,
      "signupFee": 0,
      "customPeriodType": "'Days'",
      "customPeriodCount": 0,
      "trialDayCount": 0,
      "gracePeriodDayCount": 0
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Add or Update Contact (Extended

The contact's middle name.

#### Parameters
- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **overrideLists**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will override lists of contact details in update mode instead of merging them - lists, tags, emails, phones, links, addresses, photos.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

- **ignoreInvalidValues**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will save the record even if there are some validation errors.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  This is string external reference that can be passed during creation and then if sent again it will update the record.

- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **createUser**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then User will be created. Personal email will be used as User Name.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **sendWelcomeEmail**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then Welcome Email will be sent to the newly created user.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **userPassword**: `Text`
  If password is not passed then it will be automatically generated.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **drivingLicense**: `Text`

- **drivingLicenseState**: `Text`

- **isActiveMilitaryDuty**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **isUSCitizen**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **preferredToD**: `StaticDropdown`

  | Label | Value |

- **personAffiliateCode**: `Text`

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative personal email.

- **email3**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

  The contact's work email.

  The contact's other work email.

- **home_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **home_city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **work_street**: `Text`

- **work_city**: `Text`
  The contact's work city.

  The contact's work state.

  The contact's work country.

  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **facebookUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Facebook profile id.

  The contact's Instagram profile id.

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **customField1**: `Text`
  Additional custom data for the contact record.

- **customField3**: `Text`

- **customField4**: `Text`

  Pass yes if the client is employed in this Organization.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **employmentStartDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY

- **employeeCount**: `Text`

- **dateFounded**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY

- **ein**: `Text`

- **annualRevenue**: `Number`

  The company's industry.

- **company_zip**: `Text`

- **company_countryName**: `Text`

- **company_countryId**: `Text`

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **campaignId**: `Text`

- **gclId**: `Text`

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **applicantId**: `Text`

- **applicationId**: `Text`

- **ipAddress**: `Text`

- **userAgent**: `Text`

- **siteId**: `Text`

- **siteUrl**: `Text`

- **dateCreated**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **leadStageName**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **star**: `Text`
  String Value. Supports the following items: Yellow, Blue, Green, Purple, Red. Other values will be skipped.

  This is the static array from 1 to 10

- **utmMedium**: `Text`

### Add or Update Subscription

Creates a new subscription.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **productId**: `Number`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  ContactXref have to be specified and correct to look up the correct contact

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code (Unique product identifier). ProductCode have to be specified and correct to look up the correct product
  **Required**: Yes

- **paymentPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **hasRecurringBilling**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sperse",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateSubscription",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "productId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "paymentPeriodType": "'Monthly'",
      "hasRecurringBilling": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Spotify

Music for everyone

## Actions

### Reorder playlist

Reorders items in the playlist

---


### Search

Searches for tracks, artists, albums, etc.

#### Parameters
- **search_text**: `Text`
  The word or phrase you are searching for
  **Required**: Yes

- **types**: `StaticMultiSelectDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Albums | '' |
  | Artists | 'artist' |
  | Playlists | 'playlist' |
  | Tracks | 'track' |
  **Required**: Yes

- **limit**: `Number`

- **offset**: `Number`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "spotify",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "search",
    "input": {
      "search_text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "types": "''",
      "limit": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "offset": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Stability AI

Generative AI video model based on the image model Stable Diffusion.

## Actions

### Text to Image

Generate an image using a text prompt

#### Parameters
- **prompt**: `Text`
  The text to transform in image.
  **Required**: Yes

- **cfg_scale**: `Number`
  How strictly the diffusion process adheres to the prompt text (higher values keep your image closer to your prompt) (MIN:0; MAX:35
  Default value: `7`

- **height**: `Number`
  Height of the image in pixels. Must be in increments of 64 and >= 128

- **width**: `Number`
  Width of the image in pixels. Must be in increments of 64 and >= 128

- **samples**: `Text`
  Number of images to generate (MAX:10

- **steps**: `Number`
  Number of diffusion steps to run (MIN:10; MAX:150

- **weight**: `Number`
  Default value: `1`

- **clip_guidance_preset**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | NONE | 'NONE' |
  | FAST_BLUE | 'FAST_BLUE' |
  | FAST_GREEN | 'FAST_GREEN' |
  | SIMPLE | 'SIMPLE' |
  | SLOW | 'SLOW' |
  | SLOWER | 'SLOWER' |
  | SLOWEST | 'SLOWEST' |

- **style_preset**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass in a style preset to guide the image model towards a particular style.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | enhance | 'enhance' |
  | anime | 'anime' |
  | photographic | 'photographic' |
  | digital-art | 'digital-art' |
  | comic-book | 'comic-book' |
  | fantasy-art | 'fantasy-art' |
  | line-art | 'line-art' |
  | analog-film | 'analog-film' |
  | neon-punk | 'neon-punk' |
  | isometric | 'isometric' |
  | low-poly | 'low-poly' |
  | origami | 'origami' |
  | modeling-compound | 'modeling-compound' |
  | cinematic | 'cinematic' |
  | 3d-model | '3d-model' |
  | pixel-art | 'pixel-art' |
  | tile-texture | 'tile-texture' |

- **engine_id**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | stable-diffusion-xl-1024-v1-0 | 'stable-diffusion-xl-1024-v1-0' |
  | stable-diffusion-768-v2-1 | 'stable-diffusion-768-v2-1' |
  | stable-diffusion-512-v2-1 | 'stable-diffusion-512-v2-1' |
  | stable-diffusion-768-v2-0 | 'stable-diffusion-768-v2-0' |
  | stable-diffusion-512-v2-0 | 'stable-diffusion-512-v2-0' |
  | stable-diffusion-v1-5 | 'stable-diffusion-v1-5' |
  | stable-diffusion-v1 | 'stable-diffusion-v1' |
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "stability-ai",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "text-to-image",
    "input": {
      "prompt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "cfg_scale": 7,
      "height": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "width": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "samples": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "steps": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "weight": 1,
      "clip_guidance_preset": "'NONE'",
      "style_preset": "'enhance'",
```

### Get

Get a value from storage

#### Parameters
- **key**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **defaultValue**: `Text`
  Default value: `Property.ShortText({`

- **store_scope**: `StaticDropdown`
  The storage scope of the value.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Project | PieceStoreScope.PROJECT |
  | Flow | PieceStoreScope.FLOW |
  | Run | PieceStoreScope.RUN |
  Default value: `StoreScope.PROJECT`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "storage",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get",
    "input": {
      "key": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",

    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Sub Flows

Trigger and call another sub flow.

## Actions

### Call Flow

Call another sub flow

#### Parameters
- **mode**: `StaticDropdown`
  Choose Simple for key-value or Advanced for JSON.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Simple | 'simple' |
  | Advanced | 'advanced' |
  Default value: `'simple'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **flowProps**: `DynamicProperties`
  Default value: `(castedFlowValue.exampleData`
  **Required**: Yes

- **waitForResponse**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`

- **testingProps**: `DynamicProperties`
  Default value: `{`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sub-flows",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "callFlow",
    "input": {
      "mode": "'simple'",
      "flowProps": "(castedFlowValue.exampleData",
      "waitForResponse": false,
      "testingProps": "{"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Return Response

Return response to the original flow

#### Parameters
- **mode**: `StaticDropdown`
  Choose Simple for key-value or Advanced for JSON.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Simple | 'simple' |
  | Advanced | 'advanced' |
  Default value: `'simple'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **response**: `DynamicProperties`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "sub-flows",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "returnResponse",
    "input": {
      "mode": "'simple'",
      "response": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

#### Parameters
- **mode**: `StaticDropdown`
  Choose Simple for key-value or Advanced for JSON.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Simple | 'simple' |
  | Advanced | 'advanced' |

  The schema to be passed to the flow
  **Required**: Yes

# Supadata

YouTube Transcripts

## Actions

### Get Transcript

Fetches transcript of a YouTube video.

#### Parameters
- **url**: `Text`
  The URL of a single YouTube video.
  **Required**: Yes

- **lang**: `Text`
  Preferred language of the transcript. If not available, the first available language will be returned.

- **text**: `Boolean`
  If true, the transcript will be merged into a single text instead of timestamped chunks.
  Default value: `True`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "supadata",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_transcript",
    "input": {
      "url": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lang": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "text": true
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Text Helper

Tools for text processing

## Actions

### Replace

Replaces all instances of any word, character or phrase in text, with another.

#### Parameters
- **text**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **searchValue**: `Text`
  Can be plain text or a regex expression.
  **Required**: Yes

- **replaceValue**: `Text`
  Leave empty to delete found results.

- **replaceOnlyFirst**: `Boolean`
  Only replaces the first instance of the search value.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "text-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "replace",
    "input": {
      "text": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "searchValue": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "replaceValue": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "replaceOnlyFirst": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### HTML to Markdown

```json
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Markdown to HTML

Convert markdown to HTML

#### Parameters
- **markdown**: `Text`
  The markdown to convert to HTML
  **Required**: Yes

- **flavor**: `StaticDropdown`
  The flavor of markdown use during conversion
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Default | 'vanilla' |
  | Original | 'original' |
  | GitHub | 'github' |
  Default value: `'github'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **headerLevelStart**: `Number`
  The minimum header level to use during conversion
  Default value: `1`
  **Required**: Yes

- **tables**: `Boolean`
  Whether to support tables during conversion
  Default value: `True`
  **Required**: Yes

- **noHeaderId**: `Boolean`
  Whether to add an ID to headers during conversion
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **simpleLineBreaks**: `Boolean`
  Parses line breaks as &lt;br&gt;, without needing 2 spaces at the end of the line
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

- **openLinksInNewWindow**: `Boolean`
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "text-helper",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "markdown_to_html",
    "input": {
      "markdown": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "flavor": "'vanilla'",
      "headerLevelStart": 1,
      "tables": true,
      "noHeaderId": false,
      "simpleLineBreaks": false,
      "openLinksInNewWindow": false
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
```

### Create Task

The task's content. It may contain some markdown-formatted text and hyperlinks

---


### Update Task

The task's content. It may contain some markdown-formatted text and hyperlinks

#### Parameters
- **task_id**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **content**: `Text`
  The task's content. It may contain some markdown-formatted text and hyperlinks

- **description**: `Text`
  A description for the task. This value may contain some markdown-formatted text and hyperlinks.

- **labels**: `Array`
  The task's labels (a list of names that may represent either personal or shared labels

- **priority**: `Number`
  Task priority from 1 (normal) to 4 (urgent

- **due_date**: `Text`
  Can be either a specific date in YYYY-MM-DD format relative to user's timezone, a specific date and time in RFC3339 format, or a human defined date (e.g. 'next Monday') using local time

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "todoist",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "update_task",
    "input": {
      "task_id": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "content": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "labels": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "priority": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "due_date": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Total CMS

Content management system for modern websites

## Actions

### Save Toggle

Save toggle content to Total CMS

#### Parameters
- **slug**: `Text`
  The CMS ID of the content to save
  **Required**: Yes

- **status**: `Boolean`
  The status of the toggle. "true" is on, "false" is off.
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "total-cms",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "save_toggle",
    "input": {
      "slug": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---


### Save Image

Save image to Total CMS

#### Parameters
- **slug**: `Text`
  The CMS ID of the content to save
  **Required**: Yes

- **image**: `File`
  The image to save
  **Required**: Yes

- **alt**: `Text`
  The alt text for the image
  **Required**: Yes

- **ext**: `StaticDropdown`
  The extension of the image
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | jpg | 'jpg' |
  | png | 'png' |
  Default value: `'jpg'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quality**: `Number`
  The quality of the thumbnail
  Default value: `85`
  **Required**: Yes

- **scaleTh**: `Number`
  The scale of the thumbnail
  Default value: `400`
  **Required**: Yes

- **scaleSq**: `Number`
  The scale of the square thumbnail
  Default value: `400`
  **Required**: Yes

- **resize**: `StaticDropdown`
  The method to use when resizing the thumbnail
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Auto | 'auto' |
  | Landscape | 'landscape' |
  | Portrait | 'portrait' |
  Default value: `'auto'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **lcrop**: `StaticDropdown`
  The method to use when cropping the landscape thumbnail for the square thumbnail
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Left | 'left' |
  | Center | 'center' |
  | Right | 'right' |
  Default value: `'center'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **pcrop**: `StaticDropdown`
  The method to use when cropping the landscape thumbnail for the square thumbnail
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Top | 'top' |
  | Middle | 'middle' |
  | Bottom | 'bottom' |
  Default value: `'middle'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **altMeta**: `Boolean`
  Pull the alt text from the meta data of the image. If set, place placeholder text in the alt text field above.
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "total-cms",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "save_image",
    "input": {
      "slug": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "image": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "alt": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ext": "'jpg'",
      "quality": 85,
      "scaleTh": 400,
      "scaleSq": 400,
      "resize": "'auto'",
      "lcrop": "'left'",
      "pcrop": "'top'",
      "altMeta": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---

### Save Blog Post

Save blog content to Total CMS

#### Parameters
- **slug**: `Text`
  The CMS ID of the content to save
  **Required**: Yes

- **permalink**: `Text`
  The permalink of the blog post. Ensure this is unique or it will overwrite the existing post.
  **Required**: Yes

- **title**: `Text`
  The title of the blog post

- **timestamp**: `Number`
  The date in unix timestamp format

- **summary**: `Text`
  The summary of the blog post

- **content**: `Text`
  The content of the blog post

- **extra**: `Text`
  The extra content of the blog post

- **extra2**: `Text`
  The extra content 2 of the blog post

- **media**: `Text`
  The media of the blog post

- **rssTitle**: `Text`
  The RSS title of the blog post

- **rssDescription**: `Text`
  The RSS description of the blog post

- **author**: `Text`
  The author of the blog post

- **genre**: `Text`
  The genre of the blog post

- **categories**: `Text`
  A comma separated list of categories for the blog post

- **tags**: `Text`
  A comma separated list of tags for the blog post

- **labels**: `Text`
  A comma separated list of labels for the blog post

- **draft**: `Boolean`
  Set to true to save as a draft

- **featured**: `Boolean`
  Set to true to save as a featured post

- **archived**: `Boolean`
  Set to true to save as an archived post

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "total-cms",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "save_blog_post",
    "input": {
      "slug": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "permalink": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "title": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "timestamp": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "summary": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "content": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "extra": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "extra2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "media": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "rssTitle": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "rssDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "author": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "genre": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "categories": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "tags": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "labels": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "draft": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "featured": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "archived": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

---
