### Get Card

Get a card in Trello

#### Parameters
- **cardId**: `Text`
  The card ID
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "trello",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "get_card",
    "input": {
      "cardId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

# Upgrade.chat

Supercharge your Discord or Telegram communities with subscription payments and membership tools.

## Actions

### Add or Update Contact

The contact's full name.

#### Parameters
- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **fullName**: `Text`
  The contact's full name.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **industry**: `Text`
  The company's industry.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work/primary phone number.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's mobile phone number.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **addressLine2**: `Text`

- **city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "upgrade.chat",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateContact",
    "input": {
      "importType": "'Lead'",
      "matchExisting": "true",
      "contactId": 0,
      "fullName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "namePrefix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "firstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "middleName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "lastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nickName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "nameSuffix": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gender": "'Male'",
      "dob": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bankCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "ssn": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "companyName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "jobTitle": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "industry": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workEmail1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "email2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "workPhone1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "homePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "mobilePhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "webSiteUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "linkedInUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "photoUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "street": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "addressLine2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "city": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "stateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "zip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "countryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "experience": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "profileSummary": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "notes": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "followUpDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "assignedUser": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadDealAmount": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "leadSource": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "channelId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "affiliateCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "refererURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "entryUrl": "{{previousStep.output_field}}"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Invoice

Creates a new invoice in the CRM.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  External Contact Reference (ID) . Will be used for looking a client

- **status**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Draft | 'Draft' |
  | Final | 'Final' |
  | Paid | 'Paid' |
  | Sent | 'Sent' |
  Default value: `'Draft'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **invoiceNo**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **date**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **dueDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  **Required**: Yes

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **grandTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **discountTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **shippingTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **taxTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **bCompany**: `Text`

- **bFirstName**: `Text`

- **bLastName**: `Text`

- **bPhone**: `Text`

- **bEmail**: `Text`

- **bCountryId**: `Text`

- **bStateId**: `Text`

- **bStateName**: `Text`

- **bCity**: `Text`

- **bZip**: `Text`

- **bAddress1**: `Text`

- **bAddress2**: `Text`

- **sCompany**: `Text`

- **sFirstName**: `Text`

- **sLastName**: `Text`

- **sPhone**: `Text`

- **sEmail**: `Text`

- **sCountryId**: `Text`

- **sStateId**: `Text`

- **sStateName**: `Text`

- **sCity**: `Text`

- **sZip**: `Text`

- **sAddress1**: `Text`

- **sAddress2**: `Text`

- **note**: `Text`

- **invoiceDescription**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **quantity**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`
  **Required**: Yes

- **rate**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **itemTotal**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **commissionableAmount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **unitId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Unit'`

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code. We will look up the product

- **itemDescription**: `Text`

- **sortOrder**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **transactionDate**: `DateTime`
  should be like this: 2024-06-11T11:11:41Z
  Default value: `getCurrentDateInISOFormat()`
  **Required**: Yes

- **transactionDescription**: `Text`

- **amount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **gatewayName**: `Text`

- **gatewayTransactionId**: `Text`

- **historicalData**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass true if this is not actual transaction. Should be False by default
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | true | true |
  | false | false |
  Default value: `False`
  **Required**: Yes

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "upgrade.chat",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createInvoice",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "status": "'Draft'",
      "invoiceNo": 0,
      "date": "getCurrentDateInISOFormat()",
      "dueDate": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "grandTotal": 0,
      "discountTotal": 0,
      "shippingTotal": 0,
      "taxTotal": 0,
      "bCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bFirstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bCity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bZip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "bAddress2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCompany": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sFirstName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sLastName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sPhone": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sEmail": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCountryId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sStateName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sCity": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sZip": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sAddress1": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sAddress2": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "note": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "invoiceDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "quantity": 0,
      "rate": 0,
      "itemTotal": 0,
      "commissionableAmount": 0,
      "unitId": "'Unit'",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "itemDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "sortOrder": 0,
      "transactionDate": "getCurrentDateInISOFormat()",
      "transactionDescription": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "amount": 0,
      "gatewayName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "gatewayTransactionId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "historicalData": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Create Product

Creates a new product in the CRM

#### Parameters
- **productType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | General | 'General' |
  | Event | 'Event' |
  | Subscription | 'Subscription' |
  | Digital | 'Digital' |
  Default value: `'General'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **name**: `Text`
  **Required**: Yes

- **code**: `Text`
  Sku is the product code
  **Required**: Yes

- **description**: `Text`

- **descriptionHTML**: `Text`
  Javascript and media tags are not allowed

- **logoURL**: `Text`

- **groupName**: `Text`

- **price**: `Number`
  Required for General , Digital and Event Product Type
  Default value: `0`

- **currencyId**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | USD | 'USD' |
  | JPY | 'JPY' |
  | IND | 'IND' |
  | EUR | 'EUR' |
  | GBP | 'GBP' |
  | AUD | 'AUD' |
  | CAD | 'CAD' |
  | CHF | 'CHF' |
  | CNY | 'CNY' |
  | SEK | 'SEK' |
  | NZD | 'NZD' |
  Default value: `'USD'`

- **unit**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Day | 'Day' |
  | Feet | 'Feet' |
  | Hour | 'Hour' |
  | Kilogram | 'Kilogram' |
  | Pound | 'Pound' |
  | Month | 'Month' |
  | Package | 'Package' |
  | Piece | 'Piece' |
  | Unit | 'Unit' |
  | Year | 'Year' |
  | Zone | 'Zone' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Day'`

- **frequency**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for General and Digital Product Type
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  | OneTime | 'OneTime' |
  | Custom | 'Custom' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`

- **fee**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **cycles**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **signupFee**: `Number`
  Required for all except LifeTime or OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **customPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Days | 'Days' |
  | Weeks | 'Weeks' |
  | Months | 'Months' |
  | Years | 'Years' |
  Default value: `'Days'`

- **customPeriodCount**: `Number`
  Required for Custom or OneTime Plan
  Default value: `0`

- **trialDayCount**: `Number`
  Required for OneTime plan
  Default value: `0`

- **gracePeriodDayCount**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "upgrade.chat",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "createProduct",
    "input": {
      "productType": "'General'",
      "name": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "code": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "description": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "descriptionHTML": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "logoURL": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "groupName": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "price": 0,
      "currencyId": "'USD'",
      "unit": "'Day'",
      "frequency": "'Monthly'",
      "fee": 0,
      "cycles": 0,
      "signupFee": 0,
      "customPeriodType": "'Days'",
      "customPeriodCount": 0,
      "trialDayCount": 0,
      "gracePeriodDayCount": 0
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```

### Add or Update Contact (Extended

The contact's middle name.

#### Parameters
- **matchExisting**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will try to find an existing record using Email and Full Name and update it.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **overrideLists**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will override lists of contact details in update mode instead of merging them - lists, tags, emails, phones, links, addresses, photos.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

- **ignoreInvalidValues**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes", will save the record even if there are some validation errors.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **contactId**: `Number`
  Sperse Contact ID. Will be used for looking a client
  Default value: `0`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  This is string external reference that can be passed during creation and then if sent again it will update the record.

- **importType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Lead | 'Lead' |
  | Client | 'Client' |
  | Partner | 'Partner' |
  Default value: `'Lead'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **createUser**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then User will be created. Personal email will be used as User Name.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **sendWelcomeEmail**: `StaticDropdown`
  If "Yes" then Welcome Email will be sent to the newly created user.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `True`

- **userPassword**: `Text`
  If password is not passed then it will be automatically generated.

- **namePrefix**: `Text`
  The title used to address the contact.

- **firstName**: `Text`
  Required if Last Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **middleName**: `Text`
  The contact's middle name.

- **lastName**: `Text`
  Required if First Name and Company Name fields are empty.
  **Required**: Yes

- **nickName**: `Text`
  The contact's nick name.

- **nameSuffix**: `Text`
  Additional information about the contact e.g PhD.

- **gender**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Male | 'Male' |
  | Female | 'Female' |

- **dob**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY.

- **bankCode**: `Text`
  The contact's 4-letter personality code.

- **ssn**: `Text`
  The contact's social security number.

- **drivingLicense**: `Text`

- **drivingLicenseState**: `Text`

- **isActiveMilitaryDuty**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **isUSCitizen**: `StaticDropdown`
  Possible values are: Yes, No. If nothing is chosen that means "Unknown".
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **preferredToD**: `StaticDropdown`
  Preferred Time of Day to contact with Client
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Morning | 'Morning' |
  | Afternoon | 'Afternoon' |
  | Evening | 'Evening' |
  | Anytime | 'Anytime' |

- **personAffiliateCode**: `Text`
  Affiliate Code is used for the current person detection as a source of new leads. Alphanumeric characters, underscore and hyphen are allowed.

- **email1**: `Text`
  The contact's personal email.

- **email2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative personal email.

- **email3**: `Text`
  The contact's additional email.

- **workEmail1**: `Text`
  The contact's work email.

- **workEmail2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work email.

- **workEmail3**: `Text`
  The contact's other work email.

- **mobilePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's primary phone number.

- **mobilePhoneExt**: `Text`
  The contact's primary phone number extension.

- **homePhone**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number.

- **homePhoneExt**: `Text`
  The contact's home phone number extension.

- **workPhone1**: `Text`
  The contact's work phone number.

- **workPhone1Ext**: `Text`
  The contact's work phone number extension.

- **workPhone2**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number.

- **workPhone2Ext**: `Text`
  The contact's alternative work phone number extension.

- **home_street**: `Text`
  The contact's full street address (can include apartment or unit number).

- **home_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **home_city**: `Text`
  The contact's city of residence.

- **home_stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's state of residence.

- **home_stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's state code.

- **home_zip**: `Text`
  The contact's zip/postal code.

- **home_countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's country of residence.

- **home_countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's country code.

- **work_street**: `Text`
  The contact's work address.

- **work_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **work_city**: `Text`
  The contact's work city.

- **work_stateName**: `Text`
  The contact's work state.

- **work_stateId**: `Text`
  The contact's work state code.

- **work_zip**: `Text`
  The contact's work zip code.

- **work_countryName**: `Text`
  The contact's work country.

- **work_countryId**: `Text`
  The contact's work country code.

- **webSiteUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's company website URL.

- **linkedInUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's LinkedIn profile id.

- **photoUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's person photo URL.

- **facebookUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Facebook profile id.

- **instagramUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Instagram profile id.

- **twitterUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Twitter profile id.

- **googlePlusUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Google reviews.

- **angelListUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's AngelList profile id.

- **zoomUrl**: `Text`
  The contact's Zoom id.

- **experience**: `Text`
  The contact's professional experience.

- **profileSummary**: `Text`
  The contact's profile summary.

- **notes**: `Text`
  Additional notes about the contact

- **followUpDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS. If date is defined then new Follow Up Task will be created for this contact

- **assignedUser**: `Text`
  Preferably, Sperse User Email should be passed as it is unique within Sperse account but User Name can be also passed

- **leadDealAmount**: `Number`
  Estimated deal/opportunity amount.

- **customField1**: `Text`
  Additional custom data for the contact record.

- **customField2**: `Text`

- **customField3**: `Text`

- **customField4**: `Text`

- **customField5**: `Text`

- **companyName**: `Text`
  Name of the contact's company (This field is mandatory if the First Name and Last Name fields are empty).

- **organizationType**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | LLP | 'LLP' |
  | LLC | 'LLC' |
  | Inc | 'Inc' |
  | LP | 'LP' |
  | Partnership | 'Partnership' |
  | Sole Proprietership | 'Sole |
  | Trust | 'Trust' |
  | LLLP | 'LLLP' |
  | Other | 'Other' |

- **isEmployed**: `StaticDropdown`
  Pass yes if the client is employed in this Organization.
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |

- **jobTitle**: `Text`
  The contact's job title.

- **employmentStartDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY

- **employeeCount**: `Text`

- **dateFounded**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD or MM-DD-YYYY

- **ein**: `Text`

- **annualRevenue**: `Number`

- **industry**: `Text`
  The company's industry.

- **companyPhone**: `Text`

- **companyPhoneExt**: `Text`

- **companyFaxNumber**: `Text`

- **companyEmail**: `Text`

- **companyWebSiteUrl**: `Text`

- **companyFacebookUrl**: `Text`

- **companyLinkedInUrl**: `Text`

- **companyInstagramUrl**: `Text`

- **companyTwitterUrl**: `Text`

- **companyGooglePlusUrl**: `Text`

- **companyCalendlyUrl**: `Text`

- **companyLogoUrl**: `Text`

- **companyAffiliateCode**: `Text`

- **company_street**: `Text`

- **company_addressLine2**: `Text`

- **company_city**: `Text`

- **company_stateName**: `Text`

- **company_stateId**: `Text`

- **company_zip**: `Text`

- **company_countryName**: `Text`

- **company_countryId**: `Text`

- **leadSource**: `Text`
  The first known source the contact used to find your website. You can set this automatically and update manually later.

- **channelId**: `Text`
  The channel/medium the contact used to find your website.

- **affiliateCode**: `Text`
  The affiliate/referer partner through which the contact signed up.

- **campaignId**: `Text`

- **gclId**: `Text`

- **refererURL**: `Text`
  The webpage where the contact clicked a link that sent them to your website.

- **applicantId**: `Text`

- **applicationId**: `Text`

- **ipAddress**: `Text`

- **userAgent**: `Text`

- **siteId**: `Text`

- **siteUrl**: `Text`

- **dateCreated**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS

- **entryUrl**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **leadStageName**: `Text`
  The first page of visit through which the contact visited your website.

- **star**: `Text`
  String Value. Supports the following items: Yellow, Blue, Green, Purple, Red. Other values will be skipped.

- **rating**: `Text`
  This is the static array from 1 to 10

- **utmSource**: `Text`

- **utmMedium**: `Text`

- **utmCampaign**: `Text`

- **utmTerm**: `Text`

- **utmContent**: `Text`

- **utmKeyword**: `Text`

- **utmAdGroup**: `Text`

- **utmName**: `Text`

- **requestCustomField1**: `Text`

- **requestCustomField2**: `Text`

- **requestCustomField3**: `Text`

- **requestCustomField4**: `Text`

- **requestCustomField5**: `Text`

- **sub1_productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

- **sub1_paymentPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |

- **sub1_systemType**: `Text`
  Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

- **sub1_code**: `Text`
  Code of subscription service from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 1.

- **sub1_name**: `Text`

- **sub1_level**: `Text`
  Code of subscription service level from the Sperse CRM.

- **sub1_startDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS.

- **sub1_endDate**: `Text`
  Valid date format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS.

- **sub1_amount**: `Number`

- **sub2_productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 2.

  | Label | Value |

  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |

  Code of subscription service from the Sperse CRM. Either Product Code and Payment Period Type or System Type and Code are required fields within Subscription 2.

---


### Add or Update Subscription

Creates a new subscription.

#### Parameters
- **contactId**: `Number`
  Default value: `0`

- **productId**: `Number`

- **contactXref**: `Text`
  ContactXref have to be specified and correct to look up the correct contact

- **productCode**: `Text`
  Product Code (Unique product identifier). ProductCode have to be specified and correct to look up the correct product
  **Required**: Yes

- **paymentPeriodType**: `StaticDropdown`
  The chosen Period Type has to be set for the Product on Sperse side
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Monthly | 'Monthly' |
  | Annual | 'Annual' |
  | LifeTime | 'LifeTime' |
  Default value: `'Monthly'`
  **Required**: Yes

- **hasRecurringBilling**: `StaticDropdown`
  Available options:
  | Label | Value |
  |-------|-------|
  | Yes | true |
  | No | false |
  Default value: `False`

#### Example
```json
{
  "valid": true,
  "settings": {
    "pieceName": "upgrade.chat",
    "pieceVersion": "0.0.1",
    "actionName": "addOrUpdateSubscription",
    "input": {
      "contactId": 0,
      "productId": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "contactXref": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "productCode": "{{previousStep.output_field}}",
      "paymentPeriodType": "'Monthly'",
      "hasRecurringBilling": "true"
    },
    "inputUiInfo": {},
    "packageType": "REGISTRY",
    "errorHandlingOptions": {
      "retryOnFailure": false,
      "continueOnFailure": false
    }
  }
}
```
